[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage#installing-the-artemis-plug-in-on-google-sheets)

Installing the Artemis Plug-in on Google Sheets
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [Install the plug-in from the Google Workspace Marketplace](https://workspace.google.com/marketplace/app/artemis_sheets/951824915736)
     ([step-by-step instructions](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/install-the-google-sheets-add-on)
    )
2.  [Create a new spreadsheet](https://sheets.google.com/create)
    
3.  Start the plug-in by navigating to **Extensions** -> **Artemis Sheets** -> **Start**\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-04%20at%203.32.02%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=872a0322f47c4264c73280591cdb4fea)
4.  Once you start the plugin, the 30-day free trial will begin ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screen%20Shot%202023-03-14%20at%204.40.58%20PM.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=033d832566c252593cab6fca42a21e2f)

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage#usage)

Usage

1.  [Create a new spreadsheet](https://sheets.google.com/create)
    
2.  Start the plug-in by navigating to **Extensions** -> **Artemis Sheets** -> **Start**  
      
    `The Artemis Sheet plugin must be started this way for EVERY new sheet for security purposes` ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-04%20at%203.32.02%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=872a0322f47c4264c73280591cdb4fea)
3.  In any cell, type `=ART("ETH", "PRICE")`
4.  Congrats! YouŌĆÖre now using the Artemis Sheets plugin.
5.  Checkout more ways to use Artemis Sheets at the [Syntax and Formulas](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas)
     page or check out our [Templates](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/templates)
    .

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage#installing-the-artemis-plug-in-on-windows-excel-desktop)

Installing the Artemis Plug-in on Windows Excel desktop
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

­¤ÆĪ Info

Supported on all version of Excel from **Office 2016** or later.

1.  Install the plug-in using the Installer ([step-by-step instructions](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/install-the-artemis-sheets-add-in)
    )

| Installer links |
| --- |
| [User Installer](https://api.artemisxyz.com/static/versions/ArtemisSheetsExcelDesktopAddin_v4.3.0.msi)<br> (Recommended) |
| Machine Installer (IT Admins only): please contact [\[email┬Āprotected\]](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0e7d7b7e7e617c7a4e6f7c7a6b63677d6f606f62777a676d7d20767774) |

2.  Sometimes, Window Defender will flag the plug-in as an _Unrecognized App._ If this is the case, select _More Info -> Run anyway_

![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Jhn2-D12Xd4obDZb/images/image%20(118).png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Jhn2-D12Xd4obDZb&q=85&s=13cdf714b5e1ed2caec4bd5999d67bb4)

3.  Select **Artemis Sheets** from the Ribbon Menu

![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/images/tempsnip%20(1).png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=1071af2ce7918b95c2ccfc8fc9ed2fc6)

4.  YouŌĆÖre ready to get started with your first =ART() formula! See [syntax-and-formulas](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas)
     for sample formulas or click ŌĆ£**Insert sample formulasŌĆØ** to write your first formula.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage#installing-the-artemis-plug-in-on-mac/windows-excel)

Installing the Artemis Plug-in on Mac/Windows Excel
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

­¤ÆĪ Info

In order to use the Artemis Windows/Excel Mac plugin, you must have a **Microsoft 365 subscription**. Microsoft **does not** offer plug-in support for standalone Office for Mac purchases such as **Office for Mac 2019**.You can check which version of Excel you have by navigating to _Excel -> About Microsoft Excel -> License_

1.  [Install the plug-in from the Office Store](https://pages.store.office.com/addinsinstallpage.aspx?rs=en-GB&assetid=WA200004517&isWac=False&ui=en-US&ad=GB)
     ([step-by-step instructions](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-mac-excel-online/install-the-excel-365-on-mac-excel-online-add-in)
    )
2.  Select **Artemis Sheets** from the Ribbon Menu and then select **Show Taskpane** ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/images/tempsnip.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=a923fdaef1a9a1267cf1c9052278c216)
3.  YouŌĆÖre ready to get started with your first =ART() formula!

See [syntax-and-formulas](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas)
 for sample formulas or click ŌĆ£**Insert sample formulasŌĆØ** to write your first formula.

[Overview](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/overview)
[Syntax and Formulas](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas)

ŌīśI

Copy

    curl --request GET \

        "symbols": {

Fetch Metrics for Assets by Symbol

      --url https://api.artemisxyz.com/data/{metricNames}/

#### Path Parameters

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/fetch-metrics-for-assets-by-symbol#parameter-metric-names)

metricNames

string

required

#### Query Parameters

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/fetch-metrics-for-assets-by-symbol#parameter-symbols)

symbols

string

required

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/fetch-metrics-for-assets-by-symbol#parameter-start-date)

startDate

string<date>

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/fetch-metrics-for-assets-by-symbol#parameter-end-date)

endDate

string<date>

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/fetch-metrics-for-assets-by-symbol#parameter-summarize)

summarize

boolean

When true, calculates percent change from startDate to endDate

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/fetch-metrics-for-assets-by-symbol#parameter-api-key)

APIKey

string

required

#### Response

200 - application/json

Metric data

[List Available Metrics for Assets by Symbol](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-available-metrics-for-assets-by-symbol)
[Fetch Stablecoin DAU (Daily Active Users)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/stablecoins/fetch-stablecoin-dau-daily-active-users)

[Artemis API Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=eabd6cdca59f1a644426e686e8268e62)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=ed04938f2d4a7b7545bdc91a6abc8d35)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs)

Google Sheets Add On

Install the Google Sheets Add-On

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

On this page

*   [Follow these steps to install the Google Sheets add-on:](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/install-the-google-sheets-add-on#follow-these-steps-to-install-the-google-sheets-add-on%3A)
    

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/install-the-google-sheets-add-on#follow-these-steps-to-install-the-google-sheets-add-on:)

Follow these steps to install the Google Sheets add-on:

*   Click on Extensions -> Add-ons -> Get add-ons

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(69).png)

*   Type ŌĆ£ArtemisŌĆØ in top ŌĆ£Search appsŌĆØ text box

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(33).png)

*   Select ŌĆ£Artemis SheetsŌĆØ

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(39).png)

*   Click on Artemis Sheets add-on box

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(97).png)

*   Click on Install button

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(29).png)

*   Click on Continue

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(42).png)

*   If necessary, choose the Google account under which you want to install the add-on

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(112).png)

*   Click on Allow

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(119).png)

*   Click on Next, after the add-on was installed

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(46).png)

*   Click on Done

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(48).png) Now that the add-on was installed, you have to activate it. For this:

*   [Create a new spreadsheet](https://sheets.google.com/create)
    
*   Activate the add-on by navigating to Extensions -> Artemis Sheets -> Activate (you will have to activate the add-on every time you create a new spreadsheet)

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(79).png)

*   Launch the sidebar (Extensions -> Artemis Sheets -> Getting Started)

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(115).png)

[README](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/readme)
[Uninstall the Google Sheets Add-On](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/uninstall-the-google-sheets-add-on)

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(89).png)

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/readme#%E2%80%9Cmultiple-google-accounts-issue-detected%E2%80%9D-error)

ŌĆ£Multiple Google Accounts issue detectedŌĆØ error

Check [this](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue)
 if you see this page in the sidebar.

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/readme#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

If you have any issues with the Google sheets add-on, try the following steps as weŌĆÖve found them to be helpful in fixing most issues:

*   Hard refresh the worksheet using F5 or an equivalent key.
*   Clear your browser cache (if youŌĆÖre using Chrome, hereŌĆÖs the [instructions](https://support.google.com/accounts/answer/32050?hl=en&co=GENIE.Platform%3DDesktop)
    ).
*   Load the sidebar from the drop down menu by clicking **Extensions** -> **Artemis Sheets** -> **Open sidebar**.
*   Force a refresh in worksheet by adding or removing a column to the left of column A.
*   Try opening up a blank spreadsheet associated with your Artemis Sheet account. WeŌĆÖve found most times a new blank sheet fixes most issues.
*   Create a copy of the troublesome spreadsheet (**File -> Make a copy**).

If the issues persist, please try the following

*   Logout from your Artemis account by using the sidebar (**Settings -> Logout**)
*   [Uninstall](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/uninstall-the-google-sheets-add-on)
     the Artemis Sheets add-on
*   Clear Browser Cache
*   [Install](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/install-the-google-sheets-add-on)
     the add-on
*   Log into your account by using the sidebar

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/readme#blank-white-sidebar)

Blank (white) sidebar

This error is usually generated by a browser extension which blocks cookies or interferes with the Artemis Sheets add-on. Try these workarounds:  
_\- Install the Artemis Sheets add-on in a different browser_  
_\- Turn off your browser extensions and check if the sidebar loads_  
_\- Open google sheets in a Chrome incognito window, with cookies enabled (no extensions are loaded in an incognito window)_ Here is how you can enable cookies in a Chrome incognito window:

*   click the top right cookies button ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(134).png)
*   click the ŌĆ£Site not working?ŌĆØ link
*   click the ŌĆ£Allow cookiesŌĆØ button ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(135).png)
*   the page will reload and the sidebar will show the login page ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(137).png)

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/readme#the-only-option-in-the-add-on-menu-is-help)

The only option in the add-on menu is _Help_

This error is usually generated by a temporary Google internal glitch. A few suggestions to try:

*   close and reopen the browser
*   reload the spreadsheet a few times
*   uninstall the Artemis Sheets add-on (Extensions -> Add-ons -> Manage add-ons -> click the Artemis Sheets top right three dot menu -> Uninstall), then [clear browser cache](https://support.google.com/accounts/answer/32050?hl=en&co=GENIE.Platform%3DDesktop)
    , sign out of your google account, restart browser, sign in into google account and install the add-on
*   install the add-on in a different browser

­¤ÆĪ Info

If the above steps didnŌĆÖt fix your issues, please contact us at [\[email┬Āprotected\]](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#30434540405f424470514244555d5943515e515c49445953431e48494a)
 and weŌĆÖd be happy to help!

[Common Problems with Google Sheets](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/common-problems-w-google-sheets)
[Install the Google Sheets Add-On](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/install-the-google-sheets-add-on)

ŌīśI

Excel on Windows Desktop

Install the Artemis Sheets Add-In

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

Follow these steps to install the Artemis Sheets add-in:

*   Make sure you have a compatible Excel version (2016 and later).
*   Download the installer file (most users will need the User Installer file).
*   Locate the downloaded file on your computer (itŌĆÖs usually in your Downloads folder and it should look like ArtemisSheetsExcelAddinx.y.z.msi).
*   Make sure all instances of Excel are closed.
*   Run the file. The installer will start, and you just need to click the **Next** button.

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(18).png)

*   Installation takes only a few seconds. When complete, click the **Finish** button.

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(116).png)

*   **Artemis Sheets** menu will then be added to Excel.

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/tempsnip%20(1).png)

*   [Pulling multiple symbols and dates for a single metric:](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#pulling-multiple-symbols-and-dates-for-a-single-metric%3A)

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#%F0%9F%93%8A-=art)

­¤ōŖ =ART()
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `=ART()` function to get **time-series values** for one or more **symbols** (Tokens, Stablecoins, DATs, Crypto Equities) and **metrics** (such as revenue, fees, or price) over a specified **date range**. `=ART(symbols, metrics, startDate, endDate, order, showDates, hideWeekends)`

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#pulling-live-data)

Pulling Live Data

`=ART("SYMBOL", "METRIC_NAME")` Examples:

*   `=ART("BTC", "PRICE")` pulls the latest Bitcoin price
*   `=ART("ETH", "MC")` pulls the latest Ethereum market cap
*   `=ART("SOL", "TVL")` pulls the latest Solana TVL
*   `=ART("SOL", "DAU")` pulls the latest Solana daily active address count
*   `=ART("MATIC", "FEES")` pulls the latest Polygon fees

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#pulling-historical-data)

Pulling Historical Data

`=ART("SYMBOL", "METRIC_NAME", "DATE")` Examples:

*   `=ART("BTC", "PRICE", "2022-10-10")` pulls the Bitcoin price on `2022-10-10` (midnight UTC time)
*   `=ART("ETH", "MC", "2022-10-10")` pulls the Ethereum market cap on `2022-10-10`

­¤ÆĪ Info

For performance reasons, if youŌĆÖre a large amount of historical data, we recommend using the `ARTRANGE` function below.This will also reduce the total number of calls that count towards your daily limit in Google Sheets.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#%F0%9F%93%8A-=artrange)

­¤ōŖ =ARTRANGE()
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `=ARTRANGE()` function to get **time-series values** for one or more **symbols** (Tokens, Stablecoins, DATs, Crypto Equities) and **metrics** (such as revenue, fees, or price) over a specified **date range**. `=ARTRANGE(symbols, metrics, startDate, endDate, order, showDates, hideWeekends)`

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#pulling-a-range-of-historical-data)

Pulling a Range of Historical Data

`=ARTRANGE("SYMBOL", "METRIC_NAME", "STARTDATE", "ENDDATE")` Example:

*   `=ARTRANGE("BTC", "PRICE", "2022-01-01", "2022-10-01")` pulls the Bitcoin price from `2022-01-01` to `2022-10-01` in ascending order

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#to-pull-in-descending-order,-add-the-param-%22desc%22)

To pull in descending order, add the param `"DESC"`.

`=ARTRANGE("SYMBOL", "METRIC_NAME", "STARTDATE", "ENDDATE", "DESC")` Example:

*   `=ARTRANGE("BTC", "PRICE", "2022-01-01", "2022-10-01", "DESC")` pulls the Bitcoin price from `2022-10-01` to `2022-01-01` in descending order (so `2022-10-01` is on top).

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#to-pull-in-the-dates-associated-with-time-series-datasets,-use-the-param-%22showdates%22-additional-true-/-false-parameter)

To pull in the dates associated with time-series datasets, use the param `"showDates" (`additional True / False parameter`)`.

`=ARTRANGE("SYMBOL", "METRIC_NAME", "STARTDATE", "ENDDATE", "DESC", TRUE)` Example:

*   `=ARTRANGE("BTC", "PRICE", "2022-01-01", "2022-10-01", "DESC", TRUE)` pulls the dates and the Bitcoin price from `2022-10-01` to `2022-01-01` in descending order (so `2022-10-01` is on top).

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#to-hide-data-fields-that-fall-on-weekend-dates,-use-the-param-%22hideweekends%22-additional-true-/-false-parameter)

To hide data fields that fall on weekend dates, use the param `"hideWeekends" (`additional True / False parameter`)`.

`=ARTRANGE("SYMBOL", "METRIC_NAME", "STARTDATE", "ENDDATE", "DESC", TRUE, TRUE)` Example:

*   `=ARTRANGE("BTC", "PRICE", "2022-01-01", "2022-10-01", "DESC", TRUE, TRUE)` pulls the dates and the Bitcoin price from `2022-10-01` to `2022-01-01` in descending order (so `2022-10-01` is on top) and hides the data fields that fall on weekend dates.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#%F0%9F%86%95-=artbreakdown)

­¤åĢ =ARTBREAKDOWN()
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `=ARTBREAKDOWN()` function to get **breakdown** data, showing how a given **symbol/metric** is distributed across a specified **dimension** (for example, by chain, token, pool, or protocol). `=ARTBREAKDOWN(symbol, metric, breakdown, startDate, endDate, order, showDates)` Examples:

*   `=ARTBREAKDOWN("hype","open_interest","token","2025-10-01","2025-10-05")` pulls the **open interest** for **hyperliquid**, broken down by **token**, over the period October 1ŌĆō5, 2025
*   `=ARTBREAKDOWN("stg","treasury","chain","2025-10-01","2025-10-05","desc",TRUE)` pulls the **treasury** for **stargate**, broken down by **chain**, over the period October 1ŌĆō5, 2025, with the dates displayed in descending order

­¤ÆĪ Info

Use `=ARTINFO(ŌĆ£SYMBOLŌĆØ,ŌĆ£supported-breakdownsŌĆØ,ŌĆ£METRIC_NAMEŌĆØ)` to get a list of all available breakdowns for the given symbol/metric.

*   `=ARTINFO(ŌĆ£hypeŌĆØ,ŌĆ£supported-breakdownsŌĆØ,ŌĆ£open_interestŌĆØ)` returns `TOKEN, TOKEN_TYPE`
*   `=ARTINFO(ŌĆ£stgŌĆØ,ŌĆ£supported-breakdownsŌĆØ,ŌĆ£treasuryŌĆØ)` returns `TOKEN, CHAIN`

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#%E2%84%B9%EF%B8%8F-=artinfo)

Ōä╣’ĖÅ =ARTINFO()
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#overview)

Overview

`ARTINFO()` is a flexible lookup function used to retrieve information about assets, categories, metrics, market-cap rankings, and supported analytical structures. It can perform both broad queries across the entire asset universe and detailed lookups for a specific symbol.

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#function-signature)

Function Signature

`ARTINFO(param1, param2, param3?, param4?)`

*   **param1** ŌĆö Defines query scope (`"all"`, a specific symbol, or a category for top-N queries).
*   **param2** ŌĆö Specifies the information type to retrieve.
*   **param3** ŌĆö Optional modifier (meaning depends on the query type).
*   **param4** ŌĆö Optional comma-separated list of symbols to exclude.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#parameter-definitions)

Parameter Definitions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#param1-%E2%80%94-scope-selector)

**param1 ŌĆö Scope Selector**

Accepts:

*   `"all"` ŌĆö Query across the entire asset universe.
*   `<symbol>` ŌĆö A specific asset symbol (e.g., `"btc"`, `"uni"`, `"osmo"`).
*   `<category>` ŌĆö Used only for `"topN-symbols"` queries (e.g., `"defi"`, `"stablecoin"`).

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#param2-%E2%80%94-information-type)

**param2 ŌĆö Information Type**

Valid values depend on `param1`.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#when-param1-=-%22all%22:)

When `param1 = "all"`:

*   `"symbols"` ŌĆö All asset symbols + names.
*   `"topN-symbols"` ŌĆö Top N symbols by market cap (e.g., `"top100-symbols"`).
*   `"metrics"` ŌĆö All metric identifiers + descriptions.
*   `"categories"` ŌĆö All asset categories.
*   `"equities"` ŌĆö All equity tickers + names.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#when-param1-=-%3Csymbol%3E:)

When `param1 = <symbol>`:

Returns the related property for that symbol:

*   `"asset-name"`
*   `"categories"`
*   `"sub-categories"`
*   `"coingecko-id"`
*   `"mc-rank"`
*   `"supported-metrics"`
*   `"supported-breakdowns"` ŌåÆ requires `param3 = <metric name>`

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#param3-%E2%80%94-optional-modifier)

**param3 ŌĆö Optional Modifier**

Depends on `param2`:

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#if-param2-=-%22topn-symbols%22:)

If `param2 = "topN-symbols"`:

*   `TRUE` / `"TRUE"`  
    Apply default filters:
    *   Exclude `"stablecoin"`
    *   Exclude `"staked, bridged, or wrapped asset"`
*   `FALSE` or omitted  
    No category filtering.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#if-param2-=-%22supported-breakdowns%22:)

If `param2 = "supported-breakdowns"`:

*   Must be the metric name (e.g., `"open_interest"`).

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#param4-%E2%80%94-optional-exclusion-list)

**param4 ŌĆö Optional Exclusion List**

A comma-separated list of symbols to exclude.  
Example: `"TUSD,USDC,$RCGE"` Used only with `"topN-symbols"`.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#behavioral-rules)

Behavioral Rules
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#when-param1-=-%22all%22)

**When `param1 = "all"`**

*   `"symbols"` ŌåÆ Returns all symbols + names.
*   `"topN-symbols"` ŌåÆ Returns top N by market cap  
    Processing order:
    1.  Apply default filters if `param3 = TRUE`
    2.  Remove any symbols in `param4`
*   `"metrics"` ŌåÆ Returns all metric identifiers + descriptions
*   `"categories"` ŌåÆ Returns all categories
*   `"equities"` ŌåÆ Returns all equity symbols + names

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#when-param1-is-a-specific-symbol)

**When `param1` is a specific symbol**

Return the requested data for that symbol:

| `param2` | Returned Value |
| --- | --- |
| `"asset-name"` | Asset display name |
| `"categories"` | Primary category |
| `"sub-categories"` | Sub-category list |
| `"coingecko-id"` | Coingecko identifier |
| `"mc-rank"` | Current market cap rank |
| `"supported-metrics"` | Metrics available for this asset |
| `"supported-breakdowns"` | Breakdown list for the metric provided in `param3` |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#examples)

Examples
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `ARTINFO("ALL", "METRICS")`  
    ŌåÆ Returns every metric identifier + its description.
*   `ARTINFO("UNI", "ASSET-NAME")`  
    ŌåÆ `"Uniswap"`
*   `ARTINFO("OSMO", "COINGECKO-ID")`  
    ŌåÆ `"osmosis"`
*   `ARTINFO("all", "top100-symbols")`  
    ŌåÆ Returns the top 100 symbols by market cap.
*   `ARTINFO("all", "top100-symbols", TRUE)`  
    ŌåÆ Applies default filtering (excludes stablecoins + staked/bridged/wrapped assets).
*   `ARTINFO("all", "top100-symbols", TRUE, "TUSD,USDC,$RCGE")`  
    ŌåÆ Same filters as above, additionally removing listed symbols.
*   `ARTINFO("all", "top100-symbols", FALSE, "TUSD,USDC,$RCGE")`  
    ŌåÆ Only excludes the listed symbols; no default category filters.
*   `ARTINFO("hype", "supported-breakdowns", "open_interest")`  
    ŌåÆ Returns breakdowns supported for the `open_interest` metric on `hype`.

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#pulling-lots-of-data)

Pulling Lots of Data

`=ARTRANGE(<cells containing symbols>,<cells containing metric names>,"DATE")` `=ART` and `=ARTRANGE` both support pulling multiple symbols, metrics, and dates all at once so you can fetch hundreds of datapoints in one goŌĆö**this is great for keeping your spreadsheet performant.** Examples:

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#pulling-multiple-symbols-and-metrics-for-a-single-date:)

Pulling multiple symbols and metrics for a single date:

*   `=ARTRANGE(B6:B10,C5:I5,B4)` (see a live example [here](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1_LYhYDv5scNv_n6Aj8Lugpelov93z9AkIg_jGSDLuc4/edit#gid=0)
    )
*   `=ART(B6:B10,C5:I5,B4)`

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#pulling-multiple-metrics-and-dates-for-a-single-symbol:)

Pulling multiple metrics and dates for a single symbol:

*   `=ARTRANGE(B3,C5:I5,B43,B6,"DESC")` (see a live example [here](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1_LYhYDv5scNv_n6Aj8Lugpelov93z9AkIg_jGSDLuc4/edit#gid=709708675)
    )
*   `=ART(B3,C5:I5,B43,B6,"DESC")`

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#pulling-multiple-symbols-and-dates-for-a-single-metric:)

Pulling multiple symbols and dates for a single metric:

*   `=ARTRANGE(C5:F5,B3,B43,B6,"DESC")` (see a live example [here](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1_LYhYDv5scNv_n6Aj8Lugpelov93z9AkIg_jGSDLuc4/edit#gid=1235545109)
    )
*   `=ART(C5:F5,B3,B43,B6,"DESC")`

  
**NOTE:** you can only pick 2 out of the 3 (symbol, metric, date) as a range of cells. Otherwise, the data output would be three-dimensional and would not output correctly in GSheet or Excel.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/syntax-and-formulas#duplicate-symbols)

Duplicate symbols
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In case of duplicate symbols, use the Coingecko ID in ART formulas with the prefix `CG-` Example:

*   `=ART("CG-DEGATE", "PRICE")` pulls the DeGate (symbol: DG) price
*   `=ART("CG-DECENTRAL-GAMES", "PRICE")` pulls the Decentral Games (symbol: DG) price

The Coingecko ID can be found by using `=ARTINFO("symbol", "COINGECKO-ID")`or in the Coingecko token page, in API id field. ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Jhn2-D12Xd4obDZb/images/image%20(132).png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Jhn2-D12Xd4obDZb&q=85&s=0870b0fc6cdd993301da30f4b5eae7ef)

[Installation and Usage](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage)
[Supported Symbols](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-symbols)

*   [Chain Concentration Analysis](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#chain-concentration-analysis)
    

This schema contains comprehensive datasets for tracking Wormhole fundamental data across multiple metrics categories, including cross-chain bridge activity, fees, token supply mechanics, and market data for the multichain bridge protocol.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#available-tables)

Available Tables
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Wormhole data is available in two main tables:

*   **ez\_metrics**: Main aggregated metrics for the Wormhole protocol across all chains
*   **ez\_metrics\_by\_chain**: Cross-chain flow metrics showing inflow and outflow data broken down by individual blockchain

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#table-schema)

Table Schema
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#bridge-activity-metrics)

Bridge Activity Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | bridge\_dau | The number of daily active addresses on Wormhole |
| ez\_metrics | bridge\_txns | The number of transactions on the Wormhole bridge |
| ez\_metrics | bridge\_volume | The total volume bridged through Wormhole |
| ez\_metrics | bridge\_fees | The total fees collected by the Wormhole bridge |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#revenue-metrics)

Revenue Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | fees | The total USD value generated by Wormhole from all user-paid fees |
| ez\_metrics | fees | Total fees collected by the protocol (same as bridge\_fees) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#cross-chain-flow-metrics)

Cross-Chain Flow Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics\_by\_chain | inflow | The amount (in USD) flowing into a specific chain |
| ez\_metrics\_by\_chain | outflow | The amount (in USD) flowing out of a specific chain |
| ez\_metrics\_by\_chain | chain | The blockchain identifier |
| ez\_metrics\_by\_chain | app | Always ŌĆśwormholeŌĆÖ for consistency |
| ez\_metrics\_by\_chain | category | Always ŌĆśBridgeŌĆÖ for consistency |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#token-supply-metrics)

Token Supply Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | circulating\_supply\_native | The circulating supply of W tokens in native units |
| ez\_metrics | net\_supply\_change\_native | The net change in the circulating supply of W tokens |
| ez\_metrics | premine\_unlocks\_native | The amount of native W tokens unlocked from premine allocations |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#market-and-token-metrics)

Market and Token Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | price | The price of W token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | market\_cap | The market cap of W token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | fdmc | The fully diluted market cap of W token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | token\_volume | The trading volume of W token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | token\_turnover\_circulating | The turnover of W token based on circulating supply |
| ez\_metrics | token\_turnover\_fdv | The turnover of W token based on fully diluted supply |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#sample-queries)

Sample Queries
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#basic-bridge-activity-query)

Basic Bridge Activity Query

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Pull fundamental bridge activity data for Wormhole
    SELECT
        date,
        bridge_txns,
        bridge_dau,
        bridge_volume,
        bridge_fees,
        fees,
        price
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#cross-chain-flow-analysis)

Cross-Chain Flow Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze cross-chain flows by individual blockchain
    SELECT
        date,
        chain,
        inflow,
        outflow,
        (inflow - outflow) as net_flow,
        inflow + outflow as total_volume
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics_by_chain
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -1, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        chain, date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#chain-flow-comparison)

Chain Flow Comparison

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Compare net flows across different chains
    SELECT
        chain,
        SUM(inflow) as total_inflow,
        SUM(outflow) as total_outflow,
        SUM(inflow - outflow) as net_flow,
        SUM(inflow + outflow) as total_volume
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics_by_chain
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    GROUP BY
        chain
    ORDER BY
        total_volume DESC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#bridge-usage-efficiency)

Bridge Usage Efficiency

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze bridge usage efficiency and fee structure
    SELECT
        date,
        bridge_volume,
        bridge_fees,
        bridge_txns,
        bridge_dau,
        bridge_fees / NULLIF(bridge_volume, 0) * 100 as fee_percentage,
        bridge_volume / NULLIF(bridge_txns, 0) as avg_volume_per_txn,
        bridge_volume / NULLIF(bridge_dau, 0) as avg_volume_per_user
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -2, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND bridge_volume > 0
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#token-supply-analysis)

Token Supply Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track Wormhole token supply changes and unlocks
    SELECT
        date,
        circulating_supply_native,
        net_supply_change_native,
        premine_unlocks_native,
        price,
        market_cap,
        fdmc
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -6, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#market-performance-analysis)

Market Performance Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Wormhole token market performance
    SELECT
        date,
        price,
        market_cap,
        fdmc,
        token_volume,
        token_turnover_circulating,
        token_turnover_fdv,
        bridge_volume,
        token_volume / NULLIF(bridge_volume, 0) * 100 as token_vs_bridge_volume_ratio
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#daily-bridge-metrics-summary)

Daily Bridge Metrics Summary

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Comprehensive daily bridge performance summary
    SELECT
        date,
        bridge_dau,
        bridge_txns,
        bridge_volume,
        bridge_fees,
        fees,
        bridge_txns / NULLIF(bridge_dau, 0) as txns_per_user,
        bridge_fees / NULLIF(bridge_txns, 0) as avg_fee_per_txn
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(week, -4, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date DESC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#top-chain-activity)

Top Chain Activity

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Identify most active chains by volume over time
    SELECT
        date,
        chain,
        inflow + outflow as total_volume,
        inflow,
        outflow,
        CASE
            WHEN inflow > outflow THEN 'Net Inflow'
            WHEN outflow > inflow THEN 'Net Outflow'
            ELSE 'Balanced'
        END as flow_direction
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics_by_chain
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(week, -2, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date DESC, total_volume DESC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#bridge-adoption-trends)

Bridge Adoption Trends

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track bridge adoption and growth trends
    SELECT
        date,
        bridge_dau,
        bridge_txns,
        bridge_volume,
        LAG(bridge_dau, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date) as bridge_dau_7d_ago,
        LAG(bridge_volume, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date) as bridge_volume_7d_ago,
        (bridge_dau - LAG(bridge_dau, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date)) / NULLIF(LAG(bridge_dau, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date), 0) * 100 as dau_growth_7d,
        (bridge_volume - LAG(bridge_volume, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date)) / NULLIF(LAG(bridge_volume, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date), 0) * 100 as volume_growth_7d
    FROM
        art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -2, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/wormhole#chain-concentration-analysis)

Chain Concentration Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze volume concentration across different chains
    WITH chain_totals AS (
        SELECT
            chain,
            SUM(inflow + outflow) as total_volume
        FROM
            art_share.wormhole.ez_metrics_by_chain
        WHERE
            date >= DATEADD(month, -1, CURRENT_DATE())
        GROUP BY
            chain
    ),
    total_volume AS (
        SELECT SUM(total_volume) as grand_total
        FROM chain_totals
    )
    SELECT
        ct.chain,
        ct.total_volume,
        ct.total_volume / tv.grand_total * 100 as volume_percentage,
        SUM(ct.total_volume / tv.grand_total * 100) OVER (ORDER BY ct.total_volume DESC) as cumulative_percentage
    FROM
        chain_totals ct
    CROSS JOIN
        total_volume tv
    ORDER BY
        ct.total_volume DESC
    

[Uniswap](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/uniswap)
[Overview](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-terminal/overview)

Aave

*   [Protocol Economics Analysis](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#protocol-economics-analysis)
    

This schema contains comprehensive datasets for tracking Aave fundamental data across multiple metrics categories, including lending activity, deposits, loans, revenue streams, treasury, liquidations, and market data.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#available-tables)

Available Tables
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Aave data is available in several tables:

*   **ez\_metrics**: Main aggregated metrics for the entire Aave protocol
*   **ez\_metrics\_by\_chain**: Metrics broken down by blockchain (Ethereum, Arbitrum, Optimism, etc.)
*   **ez\_metrics\_by\_token**: Metrics broken down by token (USDC, ETH, AAVE, etc.)

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#table-schema)

Table Schema
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#lending-activity-metrics)

Lending Activity Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | lending\_deposits | The total amount of tokens deposited (in USD) on Aave |
| ez\_metrics | lending\_loans | The total outstanding loans (in USD) on Aave |
| ez\_metrics | net\_deposits | Legacy naming for lending\_deposits |
| ez\_metrics | outstanding\_supply | Legacy naming for lending\_loans |
| ez\_metrics | tvl | The total value locked in Aave (deposits - loans) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#fee-and-revenue-metrics)

Fee and Revenue Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | fees | The total USD value generated from all user-paid fees |
| ez\_metrics | interest\_rate\_fees | Interest fees paid by borrowers on loans |
| ez\_metrics | flashloan\_fees | Fees generated from flash loans |
| ez\_metrics | gho\_fees | Fees generated from GHO stablecoin operations |
| ez\_metrics | fees | Legacy naming for total fees (interest + flashloan + gho) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#revenue-distribution-metrics)

Revenue Distribution Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | service\_fee\_allocation | Revenue accrued to liquidity providers (deposit revenue + flashloan) |
| ez\_metrics | liquidator\_fee\_allocation | Revenue allocated to liquidators |
| ez\_metrics | treasury\_fee\_allocation | Revenue allocated to Aave treasury (reserve factor + dao + gho) |
| ez\_metrics | reserve\_factor\_treasury\_fee\_allocation | Portion of interest fees sent to treasury via reserve factor |
| ez\_metrics | dao\_treasury\_fee\_allocation | Revenue from DAO trading activities |
| ez\_metrics | gho\_treasury\_fee\_allocation | Revenue from GHO operations sent to treasury |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#incentives-and-expenses)

Incentives and Expenses

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | ecosystem\_incentives | Incentives distributed to ecosystem participants |
| ez\_metrics | safety\_incentives | Incentives distributed for the safety module |
| ez\_metrics | token\_incentives | Total token incentives (ecosystem + safety) |
| ez\_metrics | total\_expenses | Total protocol expenses (currently just token incentives) |
| ez\_metrics | protocol\_earnings | Protocol revenue minus total expenses |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#treasury-metrics)

Treasury Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | treasury | The total USD value in AaveŌĆÖs treasury |
| ez\_metrics | treasury\_native | The USD value of AAVE tokens in the treasury |
| ez\_metrics | net\_treasury | The USD value in treasury excluding protocolŌĆÖs own tokens |
| ez\_metrics | treasury\_value | Legacy naming for treasury |
| ez\_metrics | treasury\_value\_native | Legacy naming for treasury\_native |
| ez\_metrics | net\_treasury\_value | Legacy naming for net\_treasury |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#market-and-token-metrics)

Market and Token Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | price | The price of AAVE token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | market\_cap | The market cap of AAVE token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | fdmc | The fully diluted market cap of AAVE token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | token\_volume | The trading volume of AAVE token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | token\_turnover\_circulating | The turnover of AAVE based on circulating supply |
| ez\_metrics | token\_turnover\_fdv | The turnover of AAVE based on fully diluted valuation |
| ez\_metrics | token\_holder\_count | The number of unique AAVE token holders |
| ez\_metrics | h24\_volume | The 24-hour trading volume of AAVE (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#chain-specific-metrics-ez-metrics-by-chain)

Chain-specific Metrics (ez\_metrics\_by\_chain)

The `ez_metrics_by_chain` table provides the same metrics as the main table but broken down by blockchain network:

| Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| date | The date of the recorded metrics |
| chain | The blockchain (Ethereum, Arbitrum, Optimism, etc.) |
| lending\_deposits | Total deposits on this chain |
| lending\_loans | Outstanding loans on this chain |
| tvl | Total value locked on this chain |
| fees | Total protocol revenue on this chain |
| service\_fee\_allocation | Revenue to liquidity providers on this chain |
| liquidator\_fee\_allocation | Revenue to liquidators on this chain |
| treasury\_fee\_allocation | Revenue to treasury on this chain |
| treasury | Treasury value associated with this chain |
| treasury\_native | AAVE token value in treasury for this chain |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#token-specific-metrics-ez-metrics-by-token)

Token-specific Metrics (ez\_metrics\_by\_token)

The `ez_metrics_by_token` table breaks down metrics by individual tokens:

| Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| date | The date of the recorded metrics |
| chain | The blockchain where the token is used |
| token\_address | The contract address of the token |
| lending\_deposits | Deposits of this specific token (USD) |
| lending\_deposits\_native | Deposits of this token in native units |
| lending\_loans | Loans of this specific token (USD) |
| lending\_loans\_native | Loans of this token in native units |
| tvl | TVL for this token (USD) |
| tvl\_native | TVL for this token in native units |
| fees | Revenue generated by this token (USD) |
| fees\_native | Revenue generated by this token in native units |
| service\_fee\_allocation | Revenue to liquidity providers from this token |
| service\_fee\_allocation\_native | Revenue to LPs in native token units |
| liquidator\_fee\_allocation | Revenue to liquidators from this token |
| liquidator\_fee\_allocation\_native | Revenue to liquidators in native token units |
| treasury\_fee\_allocation | Revenue to treasury from this token |
| treasury\_fee\_allocation\_native | Revenue to treasury in native token units |
| treasury | Treasury holdings of this token (USD) |
| treasury\_native | Treasury holdings in native token units |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#sample-queries)

Sample Queries
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#basic-protocol-activity-query)

Basic Protocol Activity Query

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Pull fundamental lending data for Aave
    SELECT
        date,
        lending_deposits,
        lending_loans,
        tvl,
        price
    FROM
        art_share.aave.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#revenue-analysis)

Revenue Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Aave revenue streams
    SELECT
        date,
        fees,
        interest_rate_fees,
        flashloan_fees,
        gho_fees,
        service_fee_allocation,
        liquidator_fee_allocation,
        treasury_fee_allocation
    FROM
        art_share.aave.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#revenue-distribution-analysis)

Revenue Distribution Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze how Aave's revenue is distributed
    SELECT
        date,
        fees,
        service_fee_allocation,
        liquidator_fee_allocation,
        treasury_fee_allocation,
        service_fee_allocation / fees * 100 as lp_percentage,
        liquidator_fee_allocation / fees * 100 as liquidator_percentage,
        treasury_fee_allocation / fees * 100 as treasury_percentage
    FROM
        art_share.aave.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#treasury-analysis)

Treasury Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track Aave treasury composition
    SELECT
        date,
        treasury,
        treasury_native,
        net_treasury,
        treasury_native / treasury * 100 as aave_token_percentage,
        token_incentives,
        protocol_earnings
    FROM
        art_share.aave.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#cross-chain-comparison)

Cross-Chain Comparison

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Compare Aave metrics across different blockchains
    SELECT
        date,
        chain,
        lending_deposits,
        lending_loans,
        tvl,
        fees
    FROM
        art_share.aave.ez_metrics_by_chain
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -1, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        chain, date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#token-analysis)

Token Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze the performance of specific tokens on Aave
    SELECT
        date,
        chain,
        token_address,
        lending_deposits,
        lending_loans,
        fees,
        service_fee_allocation
    FROM
        art_share.aave.ez_metrics_by_token
    WHERE
        date = DATEADD(day, -1, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND token_address IN (
            '0xa0b86991c6218b36c1d19d4a2e9eb0ce3606eb48', -- USDC
            '0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2', -- WETH
            '0x7fc66500c84a76ad7e9c93437bfc5ac33e2ddae9'  -- AAVE
        )
    ORDER BY
        fees DESC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#gho-stablecoin-analysis)

GHO Stablecoin Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track Aave's GHO stablecoin revenue
    SELECT
        date,
        gho_fees,
        gho_treasury_fee_allocation,
        gho_fees / fees * 100 as gho_revenue_percentage
    FROM
        art_share.aave.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= '2023-07-01'  -- Approximate GHO launch date
        AND date <= CURRENT_DATE()
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aave#protocol-economics-analysis)

Protocol Economics Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Aave protocol economics
    SELECT
        date,
        lending_deposits,
        lending_loans,
        lending_loans / lending_deposits * 100 as utilization_rate,
        fees,
        fees / lending_loans * 365 * 100 as annualized_revenue_rate,
        token_incentives,
        protocol_earnings,
        price
    FROM
        art_share.aave.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC

      --url https://api.artemisxyz.com/data/STABLECOIN_DAU

          ]
        }
      }
    }

Fetch Stablecoin DAU (Daily Active Users)

#### Query Parameters

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/stablecoins/fetch-stablecoin-dau-daily-active-users#parameter-symbols)

symbols

string

required

Chain symbols, comma-separated. Supports dash-separated syntax (e.g., "eth,usdc-eth,mev-usdc")

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/stablecoins/fetch-stablecoin-dau-daily-active-users#parameter-start-date)

startDate

string<date>

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/stablecoins/fetch-stablecoin-dau-daily-active-users#parameter-end-date)

endDate

string<date>

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/stablecoins/fetch-stablecoin-dau-daily-active-users#parameter-granularity)

granularity

enum<string>

Available options:

`DAY`,

`WEEK`,

`MONTH`

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/stablecoins/fetch-stablecoin-dau-daily-active-users#parameter-api-key)

APIKey

string

required

#### Response

200 - application/json

Stablecoin DAU data

[Skip to main content](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/uninstall-the-google-sheets-add-on#content-area)

[Artemis API Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=eabd6cdca59f1a644426e686e8268e62)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=ed04938f2d4a7b7545bdc91a6abc8d35)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs)

Google Sheets Add On

Uninstall the Google Sheets Add-On

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

Follow these steps to uninstall the Google Sheets add-on:

*   Click on Extensions -> Add-ons -> Manage add-ons

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(40).png)

*   Click on the upper right three-dot menu of the Artemis Sheets add-on to expand the menu

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(84).png)

*   Select Uninstall

[Install the Google Sheets Add-On](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/install-the-google-sheets-add-on)
[Multiple different Google accounts issue](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue)

# Multiple different Google accounts issue - Artemis API Docs

[Skip to main content](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#content-area)

[Artemis API Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=eabd6cdca59f1a644426e686e8268e62)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=ed04938f2d4a7b7545bdc91a6abc8d35)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs)

Search...

ŌīśK

Search...

Navigation

Google Sheets Add On

Multiple different Google accounts issue

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

On this page

*   [Why this happens](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#why-this-happens)
    
*   [Example](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#example)
    
*   [What still works?](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#what-still-works)
    
*   [Quick fixes](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#quick-fixes)
    

If you see the **ŌĆ£Multiple different Google Accounts issue detectedŌĆØ** message when opening the Artemis Sheets add-on sidebar, the issue is usually caused by having multiple Google accounts signed in within the same browser. Google does **not** support authorizing add-ons for more than one account per browser session.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#why-this-happens)

Why this happens
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When youŌĆÖre logged into several Google accounts in your browser, Google automatically marks the **first** signed-in account as your **default account**. Google then uses **only this default account** to authorize any add-on you install, including the Artemis Sheets Add-on. So even if you switch to another account and install the add-on there, Google still authorizes it under the default account.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#example)

Example
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LetŌĆÖs say:

*   **Account A** = your default account
*   **Account B** = another signed-in account

If you install the Artemis Sheets Add-on while using Account B, Google still authorizes it under Account A. When you later open the sidebar with Account B, Google checks permissions, sees that the add-on is not authorized for this account, and shows:

> **Authorization is required**

This is a [long-standing Google issue](https://issuetracker.google.com/issues/69270374)
 and has been open on IssueTracker since 2017. It is documented on Google docs page [here](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/guides/projects#fix_issues_with_multiple_google_accounts)
.

* * *

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#what-still-works)

What still works?
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can continue using **ART formulas** normally, because they run under your default account in the background. However, sidebar features will **not** work unless you use the authorized (default) account:

*   Chat
*   Formula Builder
*   Templates
*   Settings

* * *

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue#quick-fixes)

Quick fixes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Until Google enables multi-account add-on authorization, try the following:

*   ­¤ÆĪ **Tip 1:** Log out of all Google Accounts and log back in **only** with the account that has the Artemis Sheets Add-on installed.
*   ­¤ÆĪ **Tip 2:** Open the spreadsheet in an **Incognito window** and log in with the account that has the Artemis Sheets Add-on installed.
*   ­¤ÆĪ **Tip 3:** Create **separate Chrome profiles** for each Google account to avoid conflicts.

[Uninstall the Google Sheets Add-On](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/uninstall-the-google-sheets-add-on)
[Shared spreadsheet issue](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet)

ŌīśI

---

# Shared spreadsheet issue - Artemis API Docs

[Skip to main content](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#content-area)

[Artemis API Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=eabd6cdca59f1a644426e686e8268e62)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=ed04938f2d4a7b7545bdc91a6abc8d35)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs)

Google Sheets Add On

Shared spreadsheet issue

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

On this page

*   [Why this happens](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#why-this-happens)
    
*   [Example](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#example)
    
*   [What still works?](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#what-still-works)
    
*   [Quick fixes](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#quick-fixes)
    

If you see the **ŌĆ£Shared spreadsheet detectedŌĆØ** message when opening the Artemis Sheets add-on sidebar, the issue is usually caused by opening a spreadsheet owned by someone else.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#why-this-happens)

Why this happens
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you open a shared spreadsheet, the ART formulas run under the spreadsheet owner account.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#example)

Example
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LetŌĆÖs say:

*   **Account A** = owner of the spreadsheet shared with account B
*   **Account B** = opens the spreadsheet

If account A is not logged in through the sidebar, account B will see this message returned by the ART formulas:

> **Please sign in via the sidebar to use =ART functions.**

Even if account B logs into the sidebar, the ART functions still run under account A, so the same message will appear.

* * *

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#what-still-works)

What still works?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can continue using **ART formulas** as well as the Chat, Formula Builder, and Templates sidebar features normally, but they will run under the spreadsheet owner account in the background. However, the sidebar **Settings** feature will **not** work.

* * *

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet#quick-fixes)

Quick fixes
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can make a copy of the sheet under your own account. Click the **File** menu, then **Make a copy**.

[Multiple different Google accounts issue](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/multi-account-issue)
[README](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-mac-excel-online/readme)

ŌīśI

---

Excel on Windows Desktop
==============================================================================================================================================================

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/readme#common-issues)

Common issues
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

One of the most successful troubleshooting tips we use for a variety of common issues is to restart Excel. When Excel starts, the Artemis Sheets add-in checks if an update is available and it will show a message if that is the case. There is a good chance that your issue will be solved by updating the add-in. You can also manually check if an update is available, by going to **Resources -> Check for updates**.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/readme#installation)

####

Excel on Mac Online

README

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

On this page

*   [Excel on MAC / Excel online](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-mac-excel-online/readme#excel-on-mac-%2F-excel-online)
    

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-mac-excel-online/readme#excel-on-mac-/-excel-online)

Excel on MAC / Excel online
=====================================================================================================================================================================

*   Make sure that have a Microsoft 365 subscription. Microsoft does not offer plug-in support for standalone Office for Mac purchases, such as Office for Mac 2019. You can check which version of Excel you have by navigating to **File -> Account -> About Excel**.
*   ŌĆ£Centralized DeploymentŌĆØ of Office add-ins requires that the user has a valid Exchange license, as listed here -> [Determine if Centralized Deployment of add-ins works for your organization - Microsoft 365 admin | Microsoft Learn](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-365/admin/manage/centralized-deployment-of-add-ins?view=o365-worldwide)
    , so make sure you install the Artemis Sheets add-in locally and not for all users. After installation, the add-in must appear in the My Add-ins tab and not in Admin Managed tab.

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(54).png)

*   One of the most successful troubleshooting tips we use for a variety of common issues is to refresh your Artemis Sheets Add-in. This will clear your cache, update new features and platform upgrades and make sure you have the latest, stable version running. Here are the steps to clear the cache:
    
    *   Go to **Insert** menu and click **My Add-ins** button
    *   Click the upper right corner **Refresh** button
    
    ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(38).png)
    
    *   Click the Artemis Sheets add-in box (so itŌĆÖs highlighted)
    
    ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(51).png)
    
    *   Click the lower right corner **Add** button
    
    ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(28).png)

If the above didnŌĆÖt solve your issues, try to manually clear the Office cache.

*   On MAC this is done by deleting the contents of the below folders(s)
    *   `/Users/{your_name_on_the_device}/Library/Containers/com.Microsoft.OsfWebHost/Data`
    *   `/Users/{your_name_on_the_device}/Library/Containers/com.microsoft.Excel/Data`
*   On Windows delete the content of the folder `%LOCALAPPDATA%\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Wef`.
*   For Excel Online clear the browser cache.

[Shared spreadsheet issue](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/google-sheets-add-on/shared-sheet)
[Install the Excel 365 on Mac / Excel Online Add-In](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-mac-excel-online/install-the-excel-365-on-mac-excel-online-add-in)

ŌīśI

*   [Artemis Terminal](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#artemis-terminal)

*   [Artemis - Perpetuals](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#artemis-perpetuals)
    
*   [­¤åĢ Artemis - Lending](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#%F0%9F%86%95-artemis-lending)
    
*   [­¤åĢ Artemis - DEX](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#%F0%9F%86%95-artemis-dex)
    
*   [­¤åĢ Artemis - Liquid Staking](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#%F0%9F%86%95-artemis-liquid-staking)
    
*   [DefiLlama](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#defillama)
    
*   [TokenTerminal](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#tokenterminal)
    
*   [NFT Data (CoinGecko)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#nft-data-coingecko)
    

­¤ÆĪ Info

­¤åĢ For a list of all the metrics we provide, please use `=ARTINFO("ALL","METRICS")`

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#market-data-coingecko)

Market Data (CoinGecko)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   HereŌĆÖs a list of all supported symbols: [All CoinGecko assets](https://www.coingecko.com/)
    
*   HereŌĆÖs a list of all metrics we support: [All Artemis metrics](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/13ZYNCUXBScHDHPYxt0k4_fnp7phd8iNPfmgwkQDZPk8/edit#gid=264852106)
    
*   ­¤åĢ Stablecoins are also supported: `USDC` `USDT` `DAI` `BUSD` etc

­¤ÆĪ Info

For total crypto marketcap, please use `=ART(ŌĆ£TOTALŌĆØ, MCŌĆØ)`

_Note: All historical market data is fetched as of 12PM UTC_

| Name | Explanation | Period | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| PRICE | Token price | 5min | Ō£ō   |
| MC  | Market Capitalization | 5min | Ō£ō   |
| 24H\_VOLUME | 24 hour volume | 5min | Ō£ō   |
| FDMC | Fully diluted market capitalization | 5min | Ō£ō   |
| CIRC\_SUPPLY | Circulating supply | 5min |     |
| TOT\_SUPPLY | Total supply | 5min |     |
| MAX\_SUPPLY | Max supply | 5min |     |
| 30D\_VOLUME | 30 day volume | 5min |     |
| 24H\_PRICE\_HIGH | 24 hour price high ($) | 5min |     |
| 24H\_PRICE\_LOW | 24 hour price low ($) | 5min |     |
| 24H\_PRICE\_CHG | 24 hour price change ($) | 5min |     |
| 24H\_PRICE\_CHG\_PCT | 24 hour price change (%) | 5min |     |
| 7D\_PRICE\_CHG\_PCT | 7 day price change (%) | 5min |     |
| 30D\_PRICE\_CHG\_PCT | 30 day price change (%) | 5min |     |
| 24H\_MC\_CHG | 24 hour market cap change ($) | 5min |     |
| 24H\_MC\_CHG\_PCT | 24 hour market cap change (%) | 5min |     |
| ATH | All time high ($) | 5min |     |
| ATH\_CHG\_PCT | All time high change from today (%) | 5min |     |
| ATH\_DATE | All time high date | 5min |     |
| ATL | All time low ($) | 5mi |     |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#%F0%9F%86%95-equity-data)

­¤åĢ Equity Data
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

­¤ÆĪ Info

To pull stock price into sheets, use =ART(ŌĆ£EQ-COINŌĆØ, ŌĆ£PRICEŌĆØ) for Coinbase price.

**Instructions**

*   [Find the stock symbol for a stock from Yahoo Finance](https://finance.yahoo.com/trending-tickers/)
    .
    *   Examples:
        *   `SPY` for SPDR S&P 500 ETF Trust (SPY)
        *   `GBTC` for Grayscale Bitcoin Trust
        *   `COIN` for Coinbase
*   Append ŌĆ£EQ-ŌĆØ in front of the stock symbol name.
    *   Example: For Coinbase youŌĆÖd want to have `"EQ-COIN"`
*   Use the following formula =ART(ŌĆ£EQ-\[Stock Symbol\]ŌĆØ, ŌĆ£PRICEŌĆØ) to return the price of the stock
    *   Example: For Coinbase youŌĆÖd want use `=ART("EQ-COIN", "PRICE")`

**Notes**

*   Equities prices forward fill from last close on holidays / weekends.
*   [HereŌĆÖs a sample sheet using equities price](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/15OETuowc7mITQl3uLiGNnRF7c7Xg2XDaZ98H-Bv_D9M/edit?usp=sharing)
    

| Name | Explanation | Period | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| PRICE | Stock price | 5min | Ō£ō   |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#artemis-terminal)

Artemis Terminal
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Supported Symbols: all chains on [app.artemis.xyz](https://app.artemis.xyz/)
 _Note: Not all chains have all metrics listed below - check_ [_app.artemis.xyz_](https://app.artemis.xyz/)
 _for a list of chain to metric pairings_

| Name | Explanation | Update Frequency | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| DAU | Daily Active Addresses - the number of unique wallet addresses sending an on-chain transaction in a rolling 24 hour period | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| DAU\_OVER\_100 | Daily Active Addresses where the address has an account balance of >$100.**Note:** only native tokens and stablecoins are included in the account balance. | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| DAILY\_TXNS | Daily Transactions - the total number of transactions registered on-chain in a rolling 24 hour period | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| FEES | Fees paid by protocol users | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| STABLECOIN\_MC | $ of Stablecoin custodied on a chain | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| AVG\_TXN\_FEE | Average transaction fee paid by users | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| REVENUE | Fees accrued to the protocol | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TWITTER\_FOLLOWERS | Total followers on the official Twitter account | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| WEEKLY\_COMMITS\_CORE | Number of weekly commits to core repositories for a given ecosystem [FAQ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-terminal/faq) | Weekly (new data on Tuesday) | Ō£ō   |
| WEEKLY\_COMMITS\_SUB | Number of weekly commits to sub-ecosystem repositories for a given ecosystem [FAQ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-terminal/faq) | Weekly (new data on Tuesday) | Ō£ō   |
| WEEKLY\_DEVS\_CORE | Number of weekly developers for a given core ecosystem [FAQ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-terminal/faq) | Weekly (new data on Tuesday) | Ō£ō   |
| WEEKLY\_DEVS\_SUB | Number of weekly developers for given sub ecosystems [FAQ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-terminal/faq) | Weekly (new data on Tuesday) | Ō£ō   |
| WEEKLY\_CONTRACTS\_DEPLOYED | Number of unique contracts deployed to the chain | Weekly | Ō£ō   |
| WEEKLY\_UNIQUE\_CONTRACT\_DEPLOYERS | Number of unique wallets deploying to the chain | Weekly | Ō£ō   |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#%F0%9F%86%95-artemis-application-activity)

­¤åĢ Artemis - Application Activity
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Supported Applications: all applications on [Artemis Application Activity](https://app.artemis.xyz/application-activity)
    
*   Supported Categories: all category names on [Artemis Application Activity](https://app.artemis.xyz/application-activity)
    
*   Supported Chains: all chain names on [Artemis Application Activity](https://app.artemis.xyz/application-activity)
    

For symbol name for a given application, please find the associated symbol ID from [Coingecko](https://www.coingecko.com/)
 for the application (e.g symbol `UNI` for application name `Uniswap)` For chain symbol, please simply use the symbol for the given chain e.g `Ethereum` is `ETH` For category on-chain usage for a chain, please append category name-chain so `DeFi-ETH` **Examples**

*   `ART("AAVE","DAU")` returns Aave daily active addresses across all chains
*   `ART("AAVE-ETH","DAILY_TXNS")` returns Aave daily transactions on Ethereum
*   `ART("AAVE-MATIC","GAS_USD")` returns Aave daily gas usage in USD on Polygon
*   `ART("DeFi-ETH", "DAU")` returns DeFi daily active addresses on Ethereum
*   `ART("Layer_2-ETH","GAS_USD")` returns daily Layer 2 Gas usage in USD on Ethereum

| Name | Explanation | Period | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| DAU | Daily active addresses by a given application for specified chains | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| DAILY\_TXNS | Daily transactions by a given application for specified chains | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| GAS\_USD | Amount of gas spent by a given application for specified chains | Daily | Ō£ō   |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#artemis-perpetuals)

Artemis - Perpetuals
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Supported Symbols: all perpetual exchanges on the [Artemis Terminal](https://app.artemis.xyz/sectors?tab=perpetuals)

*   `VRTX`, `DYDX`, `dYdX_v4`, `RBX`, `VRTX`, `HYPERLIQUID`, `GMX`, `SNX`, `MCB`, `DRIFT`, `GNS`, `LVL`, `PERP`
*   Note:
    *   ­¤åĢ `dYdX_v4` includes `TRADING_VOLUME` , `TRADING_FEES` , `TXN_FEES` but not yet `UNIQUE_TRADERS` which is coming soon
    *   Metrics for `dYdX` are just for dYdX v3
    *   \*Currently only for dYdX\_v4

| Name | Explanation | Period | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| PERP\_VOLUME | The total trading volume on a perpetuals exchange | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| UNIQUE\_TRADERS | Returns the latest number of unique traders | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TRADING\_FEES | USDC-denominated trading fees paid by traders | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TXN\_FEES | DYDX-denominated gas fees from transactions, and USDC-denominated gas fees from transactions | Daily | Ō£ō   |

| BORROWS | Returns the latest amount of outstanding borrows | Daily | Ō£ō   |
