[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#defillama)

DefiLlama
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Supported Symbols: All chains and protocols on [DefiLlama](https://defillama.com/)
 Fees, Revenue, TVL, and DEX Volumes can be fetched by protocol version in the Sheets Plug-In. For example: `=ART("uniswap-v3", "fees")` is supported! For assets that donŌĆÖt have an Artemis ID like [friend.tech](https://defillama.com/fees/friend.tech)
, you can just grab the string after fees/ or `=ART("friend.tech","revenue")` to get revenue over the last 24 hours.

| Name | Explanation | Period | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| TVL | Total Value Locked | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| DEX\_VOLUMES | Total volume in USD through on-chain decentralized exchanges | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| FEES | Fees paid by protocol users | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| REVENUE | Fees accrued to the protocol | Daily | Ō£ō   |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#tokenterminal)

TokenTerminal
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Supported Symbols: all tokens on [TokenTerminal](https://tokenterminal.com/terminal)
 Note: pulling TokenTerminal data requires a **valid API key** generated from a TokenTerminal Pro account. This can be entered in _Extensions -> Artemis Sheets_ in Google Sheets and the Ribbon / Taskpane in Excel.

| Name | Explanation | Period | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| TT\_ACTIVE\_LOANS | Average value of outstanding borrows on the protocol | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_USER\_DAU | Daily active interacting addresses of projectŌĆÖs revenue-generating smart contracts. **Prev: TT\_ACTIVE\_USERS** | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_USER\_WAU | Weekly active interacting addresses of projectŌĆÖs revenue-generating smart contracts. | Daily | Ō£ō   |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics#nft-data-coingecko)

NFT Data (CoinGecko)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Supported Symbols: all CoinGecko NFT IDs are supported. To find an NFT collectionŌĆÖs CoinGecko NFT ID:

1.  Navigate to the collectionŌĆÖs Coingecko page. E.g. [https://www.coingecko.com/en/nft/degods](https://www.coingecko.com/en/nft/degods)
    
2.  The CoinGecko NFT ID is the right-most URL paramter. E.g., for [https://www.coingecko.com/en/nft/degods](https://www.coingecko.com/en/nft/degods)
    , it is `degods`.

| Name | Explanation | Period | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| NFT\_FLOOR\_PRICE | The lowest price for an NFT collection that someone can buy directly from the market for a given day in ETH | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_FLOOR\_PRICE\_USD | The lowest price for an NFT collection that someone can buy directly from the market for a given day in US Dollars | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_24H\_VOLUME | Total volume of NFTs traded over the course of 24hrs in ETH | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_24H\_VOLUME\_USD | Total volume of NFTs traded over the course of 24hrs in US Dollars | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_FLOOR\_MC | The lowest price for an NFT collection that someone can buy directly from the market multiplied by supply for a given day in ETH | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_FLOOR\_MC\_USD | The lowest price for an NFT collection that someone can buy directly from the market multiplied by supply for a given day in USD | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_CURRENT\_NUM\_ITEMS | The number of NFTs in the NFT collection (only available for current date) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_CURRENT\_NUM\_OWNERS | The number of owners of an NFT collection (only available for current date) | Daily | Ō£ō   |

[Supported Symbols](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-symbols)

Excel on Mac Online

Uninstall the Excel 365 on Mac / Excel Online Add-In

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

Follow these steps to uninstall the Excel 365 on Mac / Excel Online add-in:

*   Go to **Insert** menu and click **My Add-ins** button (on the newer versions of Excel click on the Add-ins button on the right of the ribbon and then click on More Add-ins bottom right button)

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(106).png) ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(1).png) Newer versions of Excel

*   Select **My Add-ins** tab

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(32).png)

*   Click the three dots top right menu next to the Artemis Sheets add-in

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(8).png)

*   Click **Remove** from the menu

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(83).png)

*   Click **Remove** in the displayed dialog

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(9).png)

[Install the Excel 365 on Mac / Excel Online Add-In](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-mac-excel-online/install-the-excel-365-on-mac-excel-online-add-in)
[README](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/readme)

Navigation

Metrics

Time Series Aggregation

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

Artemis Sheets allows you to pull in time-series metrics into a single cell. Using one of these functions would sum the requested metric across a given time period and return a value in a single cell. **Supported time frames:**

*   L7 - last 7 days
*   L30 - last 30 days
*   L90 - last 90 days
*   CM - current month (returns full calendar month for as-of-date)
*   CQ - current quarter (returns full calendar quarter for as-of-date)
*   LTM - last twelve months
*   YTD - year to date

_**Sample Syntax**_

*   _Sample syntax #1: =ART(ŌĆ£ETHŌĆØ,ŌĆ£L7\_REVENUEŌĆØ)_
    *   _The above formula would pull the sum of the past 7 days Revenue from DefiLlama._
*   _Sample syntax #2: =ART(ŌĆ£ETHŌĆØ,ŌĆ£LTM\_TT\_REVENUEŌĆØ)_
    *   _The above formula would pull the sum of the past twelve-months Revenue from Token Terminal._
*   _Sample syntax #3: =ART(ŌĆ£SOLŌĆØ,ŌĆ£L30\_REVENUEŌĆØ,ŌĆ£2025-10-01ŌĆØ)_
    *   _The above formula would pull the Revenue sum from Sep 1 to Sep 30 (inclusive). So it calculates 30 days before the given date, but excludes the passed date itself._

Note: pulling TokenTerminal data requires a **valid API key** generated from a TokenTerminal Pro account. This can be entered in _Extensions -> Artemis Sheets_ in Google Sheets and the Ribbon / Taskpane in Excel.

| Name | Explanation | Update Frequency | Supports Date |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| TT\_FEES | Total fees paid to the protocol (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_FEES\_SUPPLY\_SIDE | Fees paid to the LPs (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_REVENUE | Fees paid which benefit tokenholders (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_TOKEN\_INCENTIVES | USD value of the protocolŌĆÖs governance tokens that have been distributed to users (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_TRADING\_VOLUME | Trading volume for exchange (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_TRANSFER\_VOLUME | Transfer volume (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_USER\_DAU | Daily active interacting addresses of projectŌĆÖs revenue-generating smart contracts (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_OPERATING\_EXPENSES | Non-token costs for the protocol (for example, L1 sequencer fees for L2s) (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_EXPENSES | Operating Expenses + Token Incentives (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| TT\_EARNINGS | Revenue - Expenses (Token Terminal) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| FEES | Fees paid by protocol users | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| REVENUE | Fees accrued to the protocol | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| DEX\_VOLUMES | Total volume in USD through on-chain decentralized exchanges (DefiLlama) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_FLOOR\_PRICE | The lowest price for an NFT collection that someone can buy directly from the market for a given day in ETH (NFT Data) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_FLOOR\_PRICE\_USD | The lowest price for an NFT collection that someone can buy directly from the market for a given day in US Dollars (NFT Data) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_24H\_VOLUME | Total volume of NFTs traded over the course of 24hrs in ETH (NFT Data) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_24H\_VOLUME\_USD | Total volume of NFTs traded over the course of 24hrs in US Dollars (NFT Data) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_FLOOR\_MC | The lowest price for an NFT collection that someone can buy directly from the market multiplied by supply for a given day in ETH (NFT Data) | Daily | Ō£ō   |
| NFT\_FLOOR\_MC\_USD | The lowest price for an NFT collection that someone can buy directly from the market multiplied by supply for a given day in USD (NFT Data) | Daily | Ō£ō   |

[Supported Metrics](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/supported-metrics)
[Token Unlocks](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks)

On this page

*   [Getting a ŌĆ£Setup ended prematurelyŌĆØ message when installing](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#getting-a-%E2%80%9Csetup-ended-prematurely%E2%80%9D-message-when-installing)
    
*   [Cause](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#cause)
    
*   [Fix](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#fix)
    
*   [Getting an error message when opening Excel, after the add-in was installed, followed by scrambled text displayed in Excel.](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#getting-an-error-message-when-opening-excel%2C-after-the-add-in-was-installed%2C-followed-by-scrambled-text-displayed-in-excel)
    
*   [Cause](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#cause-2)
    
*   [Fix](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#fix-2)
    
*   [The Artemis Sheets toolbar is missing](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#the-artemis-sheets-toolbar-is-missing)
    

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#getting-a-%E2%80%9Csetup-ended-prematurely%E2%80%9D-message-when-installing)

Getting a ŌĆ£Setup ended prematurelyŌĆØ message when installing

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(65).png)

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#cause)

Cause

This happens because an error was encountered during installation.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#fix)

Fix

If you donŌĆÖt get an additional message to this (like ŌĆ£CouldnŌĆÖt find Excel location!ŌĆØ or ŌĆ£Unsupported Excel version!ŌĆØ), then contact `[[email┬Āprotected]](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ` with information about your Windows/Excel versions. If you get an additional message then check if you have Excel installed and if the version of the installed Excel is minimum 2016.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#getting-an-error-message-when-opening-excel,-after-the-add-in-was-installed,-followed-by-scrambled-text-displayed-in-excel)

Getting an error message when opening Excel, after the add-in was installed, followed by scrambled text displayed in Excel.

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(43).png) ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(88).png)

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#cause-2)

Cause

This happens because the wrong bitness add-in file is loaded (32 bit add-in in Excel 64 bit or 64 bit add-in in Excel 32 bit).

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#fix-2)

Fix

While Artemis Sheets installer automatically detects what version of Excel is installed on your computer and loads the corresponding add-in file, if you get this error it can be fixed by following these steps:

*   Check the bitness of your Excel, by going to File -> Account -> About Excel

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(45).png)

*   Open Registry Editor and navigate to `Computer\HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Excel\Options`. To open Registry Editor, type `regedit` in Windows Run prompt (Win+R shortcut).
*   Locate the OPEN / OPENx key in the right panel that points to `ArtemisSheets-AddIn-packedxx.xll`.

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(30).png)

*   If the number at the end of the file name (32 or 64) doesnŌĆÖt correspond with your Excel bitness, double-click this key and change this number to corresponding bitness. For example, if your Excel is 32 bit, change the file name in key value from ArtemisSheets-AddIn-packed**64**.xll to ArtemisSheets-AddIn-packed**32**.xll.
*   Restart Excel.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation#the-artemis-sheets-toolbar-is-missing)

The Artemis Sheets toolbar is missing

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(95).png) If you donŌĆÖt see the Artemis Sheets toolbar in the Excel ribbon, check the following:

*   Make sure the [Artemis Sheets Excel add-in is installed](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/check-if-the-artemis-sheets-add-in-is-installed)
    
*   You may need to [manually activate](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/manually-activate-the-artemis-sheets-add-in)
     the add-in

[Uninstall the Artemis Sheets Add-In](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/uninstall-the-artemis-sheets-add-in)
[Artemis Sheets Formulas](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/artemis-sheets-formulas)

ŌīśI

# Manually Activate the Artemis Sheets Add-In - Artemis API Docs

[Skip to main content](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/manually-activate-the-artemis-sheets-add-in#content-area)

[Artemis API Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=eabd6cdca59f1a644426e686e8268e62)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=ed04938f2d4a7b7545bdc91a6abc8d35)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs)

ŌīśK

Navigation

Excel on Windows Desktop

Manually Activate the Artemis Sheets Add-In

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

On this page

*   [Manually Activating the Artemis Sheets Excel Add-in](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/manually-activate-the-artemis-sheets-add-in#manually-activating-the-artemis-sheets-excel-add-in)
    

Excel needs to be configured to recognize the Artemis Sheets add-in. Typically, the Artemis Sheets installer takes care of this step automatically. There may be times, however, when the Artemis Sheets ribbon does not appear in the Excel toolbar and the user must activate the Artemis Sheets add-in manually.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/manually-activate-the-artemis-sheets-add-in#manually-activating-the-artemis-sheets-excel-add-in)

Manually Activating the Artemis Sheets Excel Add-in

1.  First, you need to know if you are using 32-bit or 64-bit Excel. Go to File -> Account -> About Excel to check which version of Excel are you using.
2.  In Excel:
    *   Click File
    *   Click Options
    *   Click Add-ins
    *   Select Excel Add-ins in the _Manage_ textbox ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(20).png)
    *   Click the GoŌĆ” button
3.  On the _Add-ins_ screen, click Browse ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(26).png)
4.  Excel Browse dialog will be displayed with the default location for Microsoft Add-ins: ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(63).png) For most installations, this is in the userŌĆÖs APPDATA folder and you simply click on Roaming (as shown).
5.  Double-click on Artemis.xyz folder: ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(41).png)
6.  Double-click on Artemis Sheets Excel Add-In: ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(109).png)
7.  In that folder, select the bit-level of the Artemis Sheets add-in that corresponds to the bit-level of Excel: ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(74).png)
8.  If you get a message asking if you want to replace the file select Yes. ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(91).png)
9.  Artemis Sheets should now appear in the _Add-ins_ list and be checked: ![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(14).png)
10.  Click OK, and the Artemis Sheets ribbon should now appear on the Excel toolbar.

[Artemis Sheets Formulas](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/artemis-sheets-formulas)
[Check if the Artemis Sheets Add-In is Installed](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/check-if-the-artemis-sheets-add-in-is-installed)

ŌīśI

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/artemis-sheets-formulas#getting-a-%E2%80%9C#name%E2%80%9D-error-in-a-cell-with-an-art/artrange/artdune-formula)

Getting a ŌĆ£#NAMEŌĆØ error in a cell with an ART/ARTRANGE/ARTDUNE formula

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/artemis-db73460d/images/image%20(122).png)

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/artemis-sheets-formulas#cause)

Cause

This happens if the Artemis Sheets add-in is not recognized / not installed.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/artemis-sheets-formulas#fix)

Fix

*   Check if the [Artemis Sheets add-in is installed](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/check-if-the-artemis-sheets-add-in-is-installed)
    . If Artemis Sheets Excel Add-in is not present, you need to [install](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/install-the-artemis-sheets-add-in)
     it.
*   If the add-in is installed, you might need to [manually activate](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/manually-activate-the-artemis-sheets-add-in)
     it.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/artemis-sheets-formulas#getting-a-single-value-in-a-cell-with-an-artrange/artdune-formula)

Getting a single value in a cell with an ARTRANGE/ARTDUNE formula

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/artemis-sheets-formulas#cause-2)

Cause

This happens if you have an Excel standalone license (not 365). [Dynamic arrays](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/office/dynamic-array-formulas-and-spilled-array-behavior-205c6b06-03ba-4151-89a1-87a7eb36e531)
 support is available only in Excel 365.

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/artemis-sheets-formulas#fix-2)

Fix

*   Use the classic [array formulas](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/office/create-an-array-formula-e43e12e0-afc6-4a12-bc7f-48361075954d)
     approach when inputting the ARTRANGE/ARTDUNE.

[Installation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/installation)
[Manually Activate the Artemis Sheets Add-In](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/troubleshooting/excel-on-windows-desktop/manually-activate-the-artemis-sheets-add-in)

# Token Unlocks - Artemis API Docs

[Skip to main content](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#content-area)

[Artemis API Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=eabd6cdca59f1a644426e686e8268e62)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=Np8G3M3xQ-5GO4un&q=85&s=ed04938f2d4a7b7545bdc91a6abc8d35)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs)

Search...

ŌīśK

Search...

Navigation

Metrics

Token Unlocks

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

On this page

*   [1\. Setup](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#1-setup)
    
*   [Google Sheets](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#google-sheets)
    
*   [Excel (Windows)](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#excel-windows)
    
*   [2\. Usage](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#2-usage)
    

Artemis Sheets allow you to pull token unlock data programmatically from [TokenUnlocks](https://token.unlocks.app/)
 directly into Excel / GSheets. ![Example TokenUnlocks Chart - Sui Unlocks](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202024-08-11%20at%204.27.19%E2%80%AFPM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=9caed2b6360bcd0998e24436117eb291) ![Sui unlocks data pulled in Excel](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202024-08-11%20at%204.31.00%E2%80%AFPM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=f7e558f6f2939aa7a6268298d23069af) **Note:** The data is provided to us by the TokenUnlocks API and aggregated weekly. We smooth it out to daily granularity to better meet the expectations of Artemis Sheets users.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#1-setup)

1\. Setup
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#google-sheets)

Google Sheets
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  If you havenŌĆÖt already, sign up for a [TokenUnlocks API plan](https://token.unlocks.app/profile)
     to receive an API key
2.  Once you have an API plan you can view your API key in [your profile page](https://token.unlocks.app/profile#my-api-key)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202024-08-11%20at%204.39.42%E2%80%AFPM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=915c31b330662df1a7a208c7a6681386)

3.  Copy the key and head over to your Google Sheets application with Artemis Sheets installed - installation instructions [here](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage)
    . Then:

![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202024-08-11%20at%204.56.17%E2%80%AFPM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=8b3abcdc459b715796592be455e38367) ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202024-08-11%20at%204.58.41%E2%80%AFPM%20(1).png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=5e10c455c23a51d15295348f6445dbab)

4.  Done! You should now see your masked TokenUnlocks API key listed under your email address.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#excel-windows)

Excel (Windows)
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  If you havenŌĆÖt already, sign up for a [TokenUnlocks API plan](https://token.unlocks.app/profile)
     to receive an API key
2.  Once you have an API plan you can view your API key in [your profile page](https://token.unlocks.app/profile#my-api-key)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202024-08-11%20at%204.39.42%E2%80%AFPM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=915c31b330662df1a7a208c7a6681386)

3.  Copy the key and head over to your Excel application with Artemis Sheets installed - installation instructions [here](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage)
     - and click on the ŌĆ£Artemis SheetsŌĆØ menu bar item. Then:

![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202024-08-11%20at%204.44.00%E2%80%AFPM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=c23d14048924b8c68cb02191bb2e32e5) ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202024-08-11%20at%204.46.48%E2%80%AFPM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=56955aa6817a49b0af7338128fe1712d)

4.  Done! You should now see your masked TokenUnlocks API key listed under your email address.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks#2-usage)

2\. Usage
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sample formula to retrieve SUI unlocks data from Aug 8th 2024, to Dec 31st, 2025: `=ART("SUI", "TU_UNLOCKS_NATIVE", "2024-08-11", "2025-12-31", "Asc", "True")` Follows the structure: `=ART(Symbol, Metric, StartDate, EndDate, OrderDirection, ShowDates)` **Metrics Available:**

*   `TU_UNLOCKS_NATIVE`: Unlocked amount expressed in the tokenŌĆÖs native units.
*   `TU_UNLOCKS_USD`: Unlocked amount expressed in US dollars.
    *   Forward looking USD unlock values use the tokenŌĆÖs price at token genesis.

Note: TokenUnlocks supports 1 year of historical data and 2 years forward looking data. Reach out to the TokenUnlocks team if you need additional data/support. You may also use the tokenŌĆÖs Coingecko ID instead of its symbol.

[Time Series Aggregation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/time-series-aggregation)
[Dune](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/dune)

ŌīśI

---

Artemis Sheets allow you to pull individual charts or queries programmatically from [Dune](https://dune.com/browse/dashboards)
 directly into your Excel / GSheets. ![Example Dune Chart - GMX Volume](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/NNkNKnlLcFniLQiw/images/image%20(80).png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=NNkNKnlLcFniLQiw&q=85&s=6195bdb92ef7389d9e9c4424547f1006) ![GMX Volume pulled in Excel](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/NNkNKnlLcFniLQiw/images/image%20(73).png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=NNkNKnlLcFniLQiw&q=85&s=48fce8fd96270e5e86082c0ac47f43c0)

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/dune#)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/dune#1-setup)

1\. Setup
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/dune#google-sheet)

Google Sheet

1.  Get your Dune API key by navigating to the [Dune API settings page](https://dune.com/settings/api)
    .
2.  Click ŌĆ£Create new API keyŌĆØ:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-04%20at%203.15.16%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=da229acc6337d780dbb96052e40cd739)
3.  Copy the new API key:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-04%20at%203.26.27%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=a408fd830d18b08adc85914c9ff4c153)
4.  Go to your Google Sheet with Artemis Sheets installed (installation instructions [here](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage)
    ) and open the side bar. Click on the settings menu:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-04%20at%203.18.38%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=7709eb143d9e0a301a6f51420d02b294)
5.  Click ŌĆ£Insert Dune API KeyŌĆØ:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-04%20at%203.19.54%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=4fef008d706ad95447c2240a7f2bf159)
6.  Past the Dune API key into the text box and click ŌĆ£OkŌĆØ:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-14%20at%204.26.48%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=11959ebefed1d145cbb8e4cad99ce8fe)
7.  Done!

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/dune#excel-windows)

Excel (Windows)

1.  Get your Dune API key by navigating to the [Dune API settings page](https://dune.com/settings/api)
    .
2.  Click ŌĆ£Create new API keyŌĆØ:  
    \\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-10%20at%205.23.39%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=f26d6e63eee9813022685380f8a5993e)
3.  Copy the new API key:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-10%20at%205.24.20%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=3e8ab74a7b59eda2385fbce32b2ee792)
4.  Go to your Excel application with Artemis Sheets installed (installation instructions [here](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/installation-and-usage)
    ) and click on the ŌĆ£Artemis SheetsŌĆØ menu bar item. Then click on the ŌĆ£External providers API keysŌĆØ button:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-10%20at%205.25.38%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=518da2c579795dc34d615dd3a04d6f01)
5.  Past the Dune API key into the Dune text box and click ŌĆ£SaveŌĆØ:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-10%20at%205.28.40%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=2ede0b106c62ab71b3e597869615ea72)
6.  Done! You should see your masked Dune API key displayed at the top right:\\ ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx/images/Screenshot%202023-08-10%20at%205.29.47%20PM.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=u2ylj6ovlda4p-qx&q=85&s=a300365e8dde7c3a1c43e1df9693d69e)

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/dune#2-usage)

2\. Usage
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/dune#1-find-your-dune-query-id:)

1\. Find your Dune query ID:

1.  Locate a dashboard from Dune youŌĆÖre interested in pulling. In the example above, we use this [GMX Everything Dashboard](https://dune.com/gmxtrader/gmx-dashboard-insights)
    .
2.  Locate a chart from the dashboard youŌĆÖd like to pull.
3.  Click on the chart title - this should take you to the [chartŌĆÖs query](https://dune.com/queries/1443379/2445683)
    . ![](https://mintcdn.com/artemis-db73460d/NNkNKnlLcFniLQiw/images/image%20(93).png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=NNkNKnlLcFniLQiw&q=85&s=e4059ffeba57d4c2ee0742cc7618fe5f)
4.  The `queryId` is the first number in the URL. For example, the GMX Platform Volume URL is: [https://dune.com/queries/1443379/2445683](https://dune.com/queries/1443379/2445683)
    . Therefore, its `queryId` is `1443379`

#### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/dune#2-syntax)

2\. Syntax

`=ARTDUNE(queryId)` In the example above, we use: `=ARTDUNE(1443379)`

[Token Unlocks](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/token-unlocks)
[Refreshing Data](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/artemis-sheets/metrics/refreshing-data)

ŌīśI

Tables

Bitcoin

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
[API Reference](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/api-reference/core-artemis-assets/list-supported-assets)

On this page

*   [Fee and Revenue Metrics](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#fee-and-revenue-metrics)
    
*   [Market and Supply Metrics](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#market-and-supply-metrics)
    
*   [Trading and DeFi Metrics](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#trading-and-defi-metrics)
    
*   [ETF Metrics](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#etf-metrics)

*   [Basic Network Activity Query](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#basic-network-activity-query)
    
*   [Supply and Emissions Analysis](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#supply-and-emissions-analysis)
    
*   [ETF Flow Tracking](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#etf-flow-tracking)
    
*   [Developer Activity Monitoring](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#developer-activity-monitoring)
    
*   [Comprehensive Market Metrics](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#comprehensive-market-metrics)
    

This schema contains comprehensive on-chain datasets for tracking Bitcoin fundamental data across multiple metrics categories, including network activity, fees, market data, developer activity, and ETF flows.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#available-tables)

Available Tables
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bitcoin data is available in the main metrics table:

*   **ez\_metrics**: Aggregated metrics for the Bitcoin network and ecosystem

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#table-schema)

Table Schema
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#network-and-usage-metrics)

Network and Usage Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_dau | Daily unique users on the Bitcoin network |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_wau | Weekly unique users on the Bitcoin network |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_mau | Monthly unique users on the Bitcoin network |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_txns | Daily transactions on the Bitcoin network |
| ez\_metrics | dau | Same as chain\_dau (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | wau | Weekly active users (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | mau | Monthly active users (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | txns | Same as chain\_txns (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#fee-and-revenue-metrics)

Fee and Revenue Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_fees | The total transaction fees paid on the Bitcoin network |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_avg\_txn\_fee | The average transaction fee on the Bitcoin network |
| ez\_metrics | fees | Same as chain\_fees (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | fees\_native | Transaction fees in native BTC (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | avg\_txn\_fee | Same as chain\_avg\_txn\_fee (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | fees | The total USD value generated by the protocol from all user-paid fees |
| ez\_metrics | fees\_native | The total native BTC value generated by the protocol from all user-paid fees |
| ez\_metrics | revenue | Total revenue (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#market-and-supply-metrics)

Market and Supply Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | price | The price of Bitcoin in USD |
| ez\_metrics | market\_cap | The market cap of Bitcoin in USD |
| ez\_metrics | fdmc | The fully diluted market cap of Bitcoin in USD |
| ez\_metrics | tvl | The total value locked in Bitcoin protocols |
| ez\_metrics | gross\_emissions | The amount of block rewards in USD value |
| ez\_metrics | gross\_emissions\_native | The amount of block rewards in native BTC |
| ez\_metrics | circulating\_supply\_native | The circulating supply of Bitcoin in native tokens |
| ez\_metrics | issuance | Bitcoin issuance in BTC (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | circulating\_supply | Bitcoin circulating supply (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#trading-and-defi-metrics)

Trading and DeFi Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_nft\_trading\_volume | The total volume of NFT trading on Bitcoin |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_spot\_volume | Total spot DEX volume on Bitcoin |
| ez\_metrics | nft\_trading\_volume | Same as chain\_nft\_trading\_volume (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | dex\_volumes | Same as chain\_spot\_volume (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#etf-metrics)

ETF Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | net\_etf\_flow | The net flow of Bitcoin ETFs in USD |
| ez\_metrics | net\_etf\_flow\_native | The net flow of Bitcoin ETFs in native BTC |
| ez\_metrics | cumulative\_etf\_flow | The cumulative flow of Bitcoin ETFs in USD |
| ez\_metrics | cumulative\_etf\_flow\_native | The cumulative flow of Bitcoin ETFs in native BTC |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#developer-activity-metrics)

Developer Activity Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | weekly\_commits\_core\_ecosystem | The number of commits to the Bitcoin core ecosystem |
| ez\_metrics | weekly\_commits\_sub\_ecosystem | The number of commits to the Bitcoin sub-ecosystem |
| ez\_metrics | weekly\_developers\_core\_ecosystem | The number of developers who have made commits to the Bitcoin core ecosystem |
| ez\_metrics | weekly\_developers\_sub\_ecosystem | The number of developers who have made commits to the Bitcoin sub-ecosystem |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#sample-queries)

Sample Queries
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#basic-network-activity-query)

Basic Network Activity Query

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Pull fundamental network activity data for Bitcoin
    SELECT
        date,
        chain_txns,
        chain_dau,
        chain_fees,
        chain_avg_txn_fee,
        price
    FROM
        art_share.bitcoin.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#supply-and-emissions-analysis)

Supply and Emissions Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Bitcoin supply and block rewards
    SELECT
        date,
        circulating_supply_native,
        gross_emissions_native,
        gross_emissions,
        price
    FROM
        art_share.bitcoin.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(year, -1, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#etf-flow-tracking)

ETF Flow Tracking

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track Bitcoin ETF flows
    SELECT
        date,
        net_etf_flow,
        net_etf_flow_native,
        cumulative_etf_flow,
        cumulative_etf_flow_native,
        price
    FROM
        art_share.bitcoin.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= '2023-01-01'
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#developer-activity-monitoring)

Developer Activity Monitoring

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Monitor Bitcoin ecosystem development activity
    SELECT
        date,
        weekly_developers_core_ecosystem,
        weekly_developers_sub_ecosystem,
        weekly_commits_core_ecosystem,
        weekly_commits_sub_ecosystem
    FROM
        art_share.bitcoin.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -6, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bitcoin#comprehensive-market-metrics)

Comprehensive Market Metrics

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track comprehensive Bitcoin market metrics
    SELECT
        date,
        price,
        market_cap,
        fdmc,
        tvl,
        chain_spot_volume,
        chain_nft_trading_volume
    FROM
        art_share.bitcoin.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -1, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC

[BSC](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/bsc)

*   [Foundation Revenue Tracking](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#foundation-revenue-tracking)
    
*   [L1/L2 Cost Analysis](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#l1%2Fl2-cost-analysis)
    
*   [Daily Performance Summary](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#daily-performance-summary)
    
*   [Revenue Breakdown Over Time](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#revenue-breakdown-over-time)
    
*   [Network Economics Comparison](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#network-economics-comparison)
    

This schema contains comprehensive datasets for tracking Abstract fundamental data across multiple metrics categories, including network activity, Layer 2 economics, revenue distribution, and fee allocation between Layer 1 costs and foundation operations.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#available-tables)

Available Tables
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Abstract data is available in the main metrics table:

*   **ez\_metrics**: Aggregated metrics for the Abstract network including Layer 2 economics and fee distribution

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#table-schema)

Table Schema
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#network-and-usage-metrics)

Network and Usage Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_dau | Daily unique users on Abstract |
| ez\_metrics | chain\_txns | Daily transactions on Abstract |
| ez\_metrics | dau | Same as chain\_dau (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | txns | Same as chain\_txns (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#fee-and-revenue-metrics)

Fee and Revenue Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | fees | The total USD value generated by Abstract from all user-paid fees |
| ez\_metrics | fees\_native | The total native value generated by Abstract from all user-paid fees |
| ez\_metrics | fees | Same as fees (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | fees\_native | Same as fees\_native (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#layer-2-economics-and-cash-flow-distribution)

Layer 2 Economics and Cash Flow Distribution

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | l1\_fee\_allocation | The total USD value of L1 fee - fees paid to Ethereum for data posting and settlement |
| ez\_metrics | l1\_fee\_allocation\_native | The total native value of L1 fee - fees paid to Ethereum in native tokens |
| ez\_metrics | foundation\_fee\_allocation | Revenue allocated to the Abstract foundation for grants, partnerships, operations, and legal expenses |
| ez\_metrics | foundation\_fee\_allocation\_native | Foundation revenue in native tokens |
| ez\_metrics | cost | Same as l1\_fee\_allocation (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | cost\_native | Same as l1\_fee\_allocation\_native (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | revenue | Same as foundation\_fee\_allocation (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | revenue\_native | Same as foundation\_fee\_allocation\_native (legacy naming) |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#sample-queries)

Sample Queries
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#basic-network-activity-query)

Basic Network Activity Query

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Pull fundamental network activity data for Abstract
    SELECT
        date,
        chain_txns,
        chain_dau,
        fees,
        foundation_fee_allocation,
        l1_fee_allocation
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#layer-2-economics-analysis)

Layer 2 Economics Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Abstract's Layer 2 economics and profitability
    SELECT
        date,
        fees,
        l1_fee_allocation,
        foundation_fee_allocation,
        l1_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100 as l1_cost_percentage,
        foundation_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100 as foundation_percentage,
        (fees - l1_fee_allocation) as net_l2_revenue,
        foundation_fee_allocation / NULLIF((fees - l1_fee_allocation), 0) * 100 as foundation_of_net_revenue
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND fees > 0
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#cash-flow-distribution-analysis)

Cash Flow Distribution Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track how Abstract distributes its revenue between L1 costs and foundation
    SELECT
        date,
        fees,
        l1_fee_allocation,
        foundation_fee_allocation,
        chain_txns,
        l1_fee_allocation / NULLIF(chain_txns, 0) as l1_cost_per_txn,
        fees / NULLIF(chain_txns, 0) as revenue_per_txn,
        foundation_fee_allocation / NULLIF(chain_txns, 0) as foundation_revenue_per_txn
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -2, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND chain_txns > 0
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#network-growth-and-usage-trends)

Network Growth and Usage Trends

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track Abstract network growth and user adoption
    SELECT
        date,
        chain_dau,
        chain_txns,
        fees,
        chain_txns / NULLIF(chain_dau, 0) as txns_per_user,
        fees / NULLIF(chain_dau, 0) as revenue_per_user,
        LAG(chain_dau, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date) as dau_7d_ago,
        LAG(chain_txns, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date) as txns_7d_ago,
        (chain_dau - LAG(chain_dau, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date)) / NULLIF(LAG(chain_dau, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date), 0) * 100 as dau_growth_7d,
        (chain_txns - LAG(chain_txns, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date)) / NULLIF(LAG(chain_txns, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date), 0) * 100 as txns_growth_7d
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -2, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#revenue-efficiency-analysis)

Revenue Efficiency Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Abstract's revenue generation efficiency
    SELECT
        date,
        fees,
        foundation_fee_allocation,
        l1_fee_allocation,
        chain_txns,
        chain_dau,
        foundation_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100 as foundation_take_rate,
        l1_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100 as l1_cost_rate,
        (fees - l1_fee_allocation - foundation_fee_allocation) / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100 as other_allocation_rate
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -1, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND fees > 0
    ORDER BY
        date DESC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#foundation-revenue-tracking)

Foundation Revenue Tracking

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track foundation revenue and operational funding
    SELECT
        date,
        foundation_fee_allocation,
        foundation_fee_allocation_native,
        fees,
        chain_dau,
        foundation_fee_allocation / NULLIF(chain_dau, 0) as foundation_revenue_per_user,
        SUM(foundation_fee_allocation) OVER (ORDER BY date ROWS BETWEEN 29 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) as foundation_revenue_30d,
        AVG(foundation_fee_allocation) OVER (ORDER BY date ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) as foundation_revenue_7d_avg
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#l1/l2-cost-analysis)

L1/L2 Cost Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Deep dive into Layer 1 vs Layer 2 cost structure
    SELECT
        date,
        l1_fee_allocation,
        l1_fee_allocation_native,
        fees,
        chain_txns,
        l1_fee_allocation / NULLIF(chain_txns, 0) as l1_cost_per_transaction,
        fees / NULLIF(chain_txns, 0) as total_revenue_per_transaction,
        (fees - l1_fee_allocation) / NULLIF(chain_txns, 0) as net_l2_revenue_per_transaction,
        l1_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100 as l1_cost_as_percentage_of_revenue
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -2, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND chain_txns > 0
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#daily-performance-summary)

Daily Performance Summary

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Comprehensive daily performance summary
    SELECT
        date,
        chain_dau,
        chain_txns,
        fees,
        l1_fee_allocation,
        foundation_fee_allocation,
        -- Efficiency metrics
        chain_txns / NULLIF(chain_dau, 0) as txns_per_user,
        fees / NULLIF(chain_txns, 0) as avg_fee_per_txn,
        foundation_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100 as foundation_percentage,
        l1_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100 as l1_cost_percentage
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(week, -4, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date DESC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#revenue-breakdown-over-time)

Revenue Breakdown Over Time

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track revenue allocation trends over time
    SELECT
        date,
        fees,
        l1_fee_allocation,
        foundation_fee_allocation,
        fees - l1_fee_allocation - foundation_fee_allocation as unallocated_revenue,
        -- 30-day moving averages
        AVG(l1_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100) OVER (ORDER BY date ROWS BETWEEN 29 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) as avg_l1_percentage_30d,
        AVG(foundation_fee_allocation / NULLIF(fees, 0) * 100) OVER (ORDER BY date ROWS BETWEEN 29 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) as avg_foundation_percentage_30d
    FROM
        art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -6, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND fees > 0
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/abstract#network-economics-comparison)

Network Economics Comparison

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Compare different periods of network economics
    WITH monthly_summary AS (
        SELECT
            DATE_TRUNC('month', date) as month,
            SUM(fees) as total_revenue,
            SUM(l1_fee_allocation) as total_l1_cost,
            SUM(foundation_fee_allocation) as total_foundation_revenue,
            AVG(chain_dau) as avg_dau,
            SUM(chain_txns) as total_txns
        FROM
            art_share.abstract.ez_metrics
        WHERE
            date >= DATEADD(month, -6, CURRENT_DATE())
        GROUP BY
            DATE_TRUNC('month', date)
    )
    SELECT
        month,
        total_revenue,
        total_l1_cost,
        total_foundation_revenue,
        avg_dau,
        total_txns,
        total_l1_cost / NULLIF(total_revenue, 0) * 100 as l1_cost_percentage,
        total_foundation_revenue / NULLIF(total_revenue, 0) * 100 as foundation_percentage,
        total_revenue / NULLIF(total_txns, 0) as avg_revenue_per_txn
    FROM
        monthly_summary
    ORDER BY
        month DESC

This schema contains comprehensive datasets for tracking Akash fundamental data across multiple metrics categories, including network activity, compute services, revenue streams, token economics, and market data.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#available-tables)

Available Tables
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Akash data is available in two main tables:

*   **ez\_metrics**: Main aggregated metrics for the entire Akash protocol
*   **ez\_metrics\_by\_chain**: Metrics specific to the Akash chain (mostly a duplicate of ez\_metrics)

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#table-schema)

Table Schema
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#network-activity-metrics)

Network Activity Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | active\_leases | The number of active compute leases on Akash Network |
| ez\_metrics | active\_providers | The number of active compute providers on the network |
| ez\_metrics | new\_leases | The number of new compute leases created |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#revenue-and-fee-metrics)

Revenue and Fee Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | compute\_fees | Fees paid for compute resources in USD |
| ez\_metrics | compute\_fees\_native | Fees paid for compute resources in AKT tokens |
| ez\_metrics | compute\_fees\_usdc | Fees paid for compute resources in USDC |
| ez\_metrics | compute\_fees\_total\_usd | Total compute fees across all currencies in USD |
| ez\_metrics | gas\_fees | Transaction fees paid to validators in USD |
| ez\_metrics | validator\_fees | Same as gas\_fees (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | validator\_fees\_native | Transaction fees paid to validators in AKT tokens |
| ez\_metrics | total\_fees | Sum of all fees on the network |
| ez\_metrics | fees | Total revenue generated (compute\_fees + gas\_fees) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#revenue-distribution-metrics)

Revenue Distribution Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | service\_fee\_allocation | Revenue accrued to compute providers (compute\_fees minus treasury portion) |
| ez\_metrics | validator\_fee\_allocation | Revenue allocated to validators (gas\_fees) |
| ez\_metrics | treasury\_fee\_allocation | Revenue allocated to Akash treasury |
| ez\_metrics | revenue | Legacy naming for treasury\_fee\_allocation |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#token-supply-metrics)

Token Supply Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | gross\_emissions\_native | The amount of new AKT tokens emitted |
| ez\_metrics | premine\_unlocks\_native | The amount of AKT tokens unlocked from premine |
| ez\_metrics | burns\_native | The amount of AKT tokens burned |
| ez\_metrics | total\_burned\_native | Legacy naming for burns\_native |
| ez\_metrics | net\_supply\_change\_native | Net change in circulating supply (emissions + unlocks - burns) |
| ez\_metrics | circulating\_supply\_native | The circulating supply of AKT in native tokens |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#market-and-token-metrics)

Market and Token Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | price | The price of AKT token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | market\_cap | The market cap of AKT token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | fdmc | The fully diluted market cap of AKT token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | token\_volume | The trading volume of AKT token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | token\_turnover\_circulating | The turnover of AKT based on circulating supply |
| ez\_metrics | token\_turnover\_fdv | The turnover of AKT based on fully diluted valuation |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#sample-queries)

Sample Queries
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#basic-network-activity-query)

Basic Network Activity Query

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Pull fundamental network activity data for Akash
    SELECT
        date,
        active_providers,
        active_leases,
        new_leases,
        price
    FROM
        art_share.akash.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#revenue-analysis)

Revenue Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Akash revenue streams
    SELECT
        date,
        compute_fees,
        gas_fees,
        fees,
        compute_fees / fees * 100 as compute_fees_percentage,
        gas_fees / fees * 100 as gas_fees_percentage
    FROM
        art_share.akash.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#revenue-distribution-analysis)

Revenue Distribution Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze how Akash revenue is distributed
    SELECT
        date,
        fees,
        service_fee_allocation,
        validator_fee_allocation,
        treasury_fee_allocation,
        service_fee_allocation / fees * 100 as providers_percentage,
        validator_fee_allocation / fees * 100 as validators_percentage,
        treasury_fee_allocation / fees * 100 as treasury_percentage
    FROM
        art_share.akash.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND fees > 0
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#token-supply-analysis)

Token Supply Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Track AKT token supply changes
    SELECT
        date,
        gross_emissions_native,
        premine_unlocks_native,
        burns_native,
        net_supply_change_native,
        circulating_supply_native,
        price,
        circulating_supply_native * price as market_cap_calc
    FROM
        art_share.akash.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -6, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#provider-and-lease-growth-metrics)

Provider and Lease Growth Metrics

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze growth of the Akash compute marketplace
    SELECT
        date,
        active_providers,
        active_leases,
        new_leases,
        active_leases / NULLIF(active_providers, 0) as leases_per_provider,
        LAG(active_providers, 30) OVER (ORDER BY date) as providers_30d_ago,
        LAG(active_leases, 30) OVER (ORDER BY date) as leases_30d_ago,
        active_providers / NULLIF(providers_30d_ago, 0) - 1 as provider_monthly_growth,
        active_leases / NULLIF(leases_30d_ago, 0) - 1 as lease_monthly_growth
    FROM
        art_share.akash.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -6, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#revenue-vs-market-metrics)

Revenue vs. Market Metrics

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze relationship between revenue and market metrics
    SELECT
        date,
        compute_fees,
        fees,
        price,
        market_cap,
        market_cap / NULLIF(fees, 0) as price_to_revenue_ratio,
        token_volume / NULLIF(fees, 0) as volume_to_revenue_ratio
    FROM
        art_share.akash.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -6, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND fees > 0
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#monthly-compute-marketplace-statistics)

Monthly Compute Marketplace Statistics

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Calculate monthly compute marketplace statistics
    SELECT
        DATE_TRUNC('month', date) as month,
        AVG(active_providers) as avg_providers,
        AVG(active_leases) as avg_leases,
        SUM(new_leases) as total_new_leases,
        SUM(compute_fees) as total_compute_fees,
        SUM(fees) as total_revenue,
        AVG(price) as avg_token_price
    FROM
        art_share.akash.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(year, -1, CURRENT_DATE())
    GROUP BY
        DATE_TRUNC('month', date)
    ORDER BY
        month ASC
    

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/akash#ecosystem-economics-analysis)

Ecosystem Economics Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Akash ecosystem economics
    SELECT
        date,
        active_providers,
        active_leases,
        compute_fees,
        service_fee_allocation,
        compute_fees / NULLIF(active_leases, 0) as avg_fee_per_lease,
        service_fee_allocation / NULLIF(active_providers, 0) as avg_revenue_per_provider,
        gross_emissions_native - burns_native as net_inflation,
        net_inflation / NULLIF(circulating_supply_native, 0) * 100 as inflation_rate
    FROM
        art_share.akash.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC
    

[Aevo](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/aevo)
[ALEX](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/alex)

ŌīśI

This schema contains comprehensive on-chain datasets for tracking Jito fundamental data across multiple metrics categories, including block infrastructure, liquid staking, fee distribution, token economics, and market data.

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#available-tables)

Available Tables
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Jito data is available in two main tables:

*   **ez\_metrics**: Aggregated metrics for the entire Jito protocol with detailed token supply and revenue data
*   **ez\_metrics\_by\_chain**: Contains key metrics broken down by blockchain (currently Solana)

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#table-schema)

Table Schema
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#block-infrastructure-metrics)

Block Infrastructure Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | block\_infra\_txns | The number of transactions on JitoŌĆÖs block infrastructure (total tips processed daily) |
| ez\_metrics | block\_infra\_dau | The number of daily active tippers leveraging JitoŌĆÖs block infrastructure |
| ez\_metrics | block\_infra\_fees | Fees generated from JitoŌĆÖs block infrastructure (tips) |
| ez\_metrics | txns | Total transactions (legacy naming, same as block\_infra\_txns) |
| ez\_metrics | dau | Daily active users (legacy naming, same as block\_infra\_dau) |
| ez\_metrics | tip\_txns | Transactions related to tips (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | tip\_dau | Daily active users for tipping (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | tip\_fees | Fees from tips (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#liquid-staking-metrics)

Liquid Staking Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | tvl | The total value locked in Jito liquid staking |
| ez\_metrics | tvl\_net\_change | The net change in the total value locked in Jito liquid staking |
| ez\_metrics | lst\_fees | Fees generated from JitoŌĆÖs liquid staking service |
| ez\_metrics | amount\_staked\_usd | Value staked in USD (legacy naming, same as tvl) |
| ez\_metrics | amount\_staked\_usd\_net\_change | Net change in staked value (legacy naming, same as tvl\_net\_change) |
| ez\_metrics | withdraw\_management\_fees | Fees from withdrawal management (legacy naming, same as lst\_fees) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#fee-and-revenue-metrics)

Fee and Revenue Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | fees | The total USD value generated by Jito from all user-paid fees |
| ez\_metrics | fees | Total fees collected (legacy naming, sum of tip\_fees and lst\_fees) |
| ez\_metrics | revenue | Total revenue (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | supply\_side\_fees | Fees distributed to supply-side participants (legacy naming) |
| ez\_metrics | tip\_revenue | Revenue from tips (legacy naming) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#cash-flow-distribution-metrics)

Cash Flow Distribution Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | equity\_fee\_allocation | Revenue distributed to equity holders (3-5% of tip fees depending on date) |
| ez\_metrics | treasury\_fee\_allocation | Revenue allocated to the protocolŌĆÖs treasury (2.7% of tip fees after March 7, 2025) |
| ez\_metrics | strategy\_fee\_allocation | Revenue distributed to entities managing capital deployment (0.3% of tip fees after March 7, 2025) |
| ez\_metrics | validator\_fee\_allocation | Portion of revenue allocated to validators (94-95% of tip fees depending on date) |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#market-and-token-metrics)

Market and Token Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | price | The price of JTO in USD |
| ez\_metrics | market\_cap | The market cap of JTO token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | fdmc | The fully diluted market cap of JTO token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | token\_volume | The trading volume of JTO token in USD |
| ez\_metrics | token\_turnover\_circulating | The turnover of JTO based on circulating supply |
| ez\_metrics | token\_turnover\_fdv | The turnover of JTO based on fully diluted valuation |

### 

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#token-supply-metrics)

Token Supply Metrics

| Table Name | Column Name | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ez\_metrics | circulating\_supply\_native | The circulating supply of JTO in native tokens |
| ez\_metrics | net\_supply\_change\_native | The net change in the circulating supply of JTO in native tokens |
| ez\_metrics | emissions\_native | The amount of new JTO tokens emitted |
| ez\_metrics | premine\_unlocks\_native | The amount of native tokens unlocked from premine |
| ez\_metrics | burns\_native | The amount of JTO tokens burned |

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#sample-queries)

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#block-infrastructure-analysis)

    -- Analyze Jito's block infrastructure usage
    SELECT
        date,
        block_infra_txns,
        block_infra_dau,
        block_infra_fees
    FROM
        art_share.jito.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC

        lst_fees
    FROM
        art_share.jito.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
    ORDER BY
        date ASC

        date,
        fees,
        block_infra_fees,
        lst_fees
    FROM

    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())

        net_supply_change_native,
        emissions_native,
        premine_unlocks_native,
        burns_native

        art_share.jito.ez_metrics
    WHERE
        date >= '2023-06-01'
    ORDER BY

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#comprehensive-protocol-growth)

        block_infra_dau,
        tvl,
        fees,
        price,
        market_cap

[ŌĆŗ](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/snowflake-share/tables/jito#chain-specific-analysis)

Chain-specific Analysis

Copy

Ask AI

    -- Analyze Jito metrics on Solana
    SELECT
        date,
        chain,
        block_infra_txns,
        block_infra_dau,
        tvl,
        fees,
        validator_fee_allocation
    FROM
        art_share.jito.ez_metrics_by_chain
    WHERE
        date >= DATEADD(month, -3, CURRENT_DATE())
        AND chain = 'solana'
    ORDER BY
        date ASC

Across

[Documentation](https://app.artemisanalytics.com/docs/welcome/overview)
